\n    def get_hash(self) -> str:\n        """Get hash of credential for caching."""\n        data = f"{self.service_name}:{self.credential_type}:{self.credential_value}"\n        return         new_credential_value = await handler.refresh(credential)\n            \n            # Update credential\n            updates = {\n                "credential_value": new_credential_value,\n                "status": CredentialStatus.ACTIVE,\n                "expires_at": datetime.utcnow() + timedelta(days=30)  # Default 30 days\n            }\n            \n            self.credential_store.update_credential(credential_id, updates)\n            \n            # Verify new credential\n            result = await self.verifier.verify_credential(credential_id, force_refresh=True)\n            return result.is_valid\n            \n        except Exception as e:\n            print(f"Error refreshing credential {credential_id}: {e}")\n            return False\n    \n    async def auto_refresh_expiring_credentials(self, hours_threshold: int = 24):\n        """\n        Automatically refresh credentials expiring within threshold.\n        \n        Args:\n            hours_threshold: Refresh credentials expiring within this many hours\n        """\n        expiring = self.credential_store.get_expiring_credentials(hours_threshold)\n        \n        for credential in expiring:\n            if credential.status == CredentialStatus.ACTIVE:\n                await self.refresh_credential(credential.id)\n\n\nclass CredentialVerificationSystem:\n calculations.\n\n<function_calls>\n<create-file file_path="murphy_implementation/validation/historical_analyzer.py">\n"""\nHistorical Data Analysis System\nAnalyzes historical data to improve UD (Uncertainty in Data) calculations.\n"""\n\nfrom typing import Dict, List, Optional, Any, Tuple\nfrom datetime import datetime, timedelta\nfrom enum import Enum\nfrom pydantic import BaseModel, Field\nimport statistics\nfrom collections import defaultdict\n\n\nclass DataQualityMetric(str, Enum):\n    """Types of data quality metrics."""\n    COMPLETENESS = "completeness"\n    ACCURACY = "accuracy"\n    CONSISTENCY = "consistency"\n    TIMELINESS = "timeliness"\n    VALIDITY = "validity"\n    UNIQUENESS = "uniqueness"\n\n\nclass DataSourceType(str, Enum):\n    """Types of data sources."""\n    DATABASE = "database"\n    API = "api"\n    FILE = "file"\n    STREAM = "stream"\n    MANUAL_ENTRY = "manual_entry"\n    EXTERNAL_SERVICE = "external_service"\n\n\nclass Field(ge=0.0, le=1.0)\n    timeliness: float = Field(ge=0.0, le=1.0)\n    validity: float = Field(ge=0.0, le=1.0)\n    uniqueness: float = Field(ge=0.0, le=1.0)\n    overall: float = Field(ge=0.0, le=1.0)\n    \n    @classmethod\n    def calculate_overall(cls, metrics: Dict[DataQualityMetric, float]) -> float:\n        """Calculate overall quality score from individual metrics."""\n        if Field(default_factory=list)\n\n\nclass HistoricalDataStore:\n    """\n    Stores historical data points for analysis.\n    In production, this would use a time-series database.\n    """\n    \n    def __init__(self):\n        self.data_points: List[HistoricalDataPoint] = []\n        self.source_index: Dict[str, List[HistoricalDataPoint]] = defaultdict(list)\n    \n    def add_data_point(self,    def get_data_points(\n        self,\n        source_name: Optional[str] = None,\n        source_type: Optional[DataSourceType] = None,\n        start_time: Optional[datetime] = None,\n        end_time: Optional[datetime] = None\n    ) -> List[HistoricalDataPoint]:\n        """Retrieve data points with filters."""\n        points = self.data_points\n        \n        if source_name:\n            points = self.source_index.get(source_name, [])\n        \n        if source_type:\n            points = [p for p in points if p.source_type == source_type]\n        \n        if start_time:\n            points = [p for p in points if p.timestamp >= start_time]\n        \n        if end_time:\n            points = [p for p in points if p.timestamp <= end_time]\n        \n        return points\n    \n    def get_recent_data_points(\n        self,\n        source_name: str,\n        hours: int = 24\n    ) -> List[HistoricalDataPoint]:\n        """Get recent data points for a data_store\n    \n    def analyze_source(\n        self,\n        source_name: str,\n        analysis_period_hours: int = 168  # 7 days default\n    ) -> HistoricalAnalysisResult:\n        """\n        Analyze historical data for a source.\n        \n        Args:\n            source_name: Name of the data source\n            analysis_period_hours: Hours of history to analyze\n            \n        Returns:\n            HistoricalAnalysisResult with quality and uncertainty scores\n        """\n        end_time = datetime.utcnow()\n        start_time = end_time - timedelta(hours=analysis_period_hours)\n        \n        data_points = self.data_store.get_data_points(\n            source_name=source_name,\n            start_time=start_time,\n            end_time=end_time\n        )\n        \n        if not data_points:\n            return self._create_default_result(source_name, start_time, end_time)\n        \n        # Calculate quality metrics\n        quality_score = self._calculate_quality_score(data_points)\n        \n        # Calculate reliability score\n        reliability_score = self._calculate_reliability_score(data_points)\n        \n        # Calculate uncertainty score (inverse of reliability)\n        uncertainty_score = 1.0 - reliability_score\n        \n        # Analyze trends\n        trends = self._analyze_trends(data_points)\n        \n        # Generate recommendations\n        recommendations = self._generate_recommendations(\n            quality_score,\n            reliability_score,\n            trends\n        )\n        \n        return HistoricalAnalysisResult(\n            source_name=source_name,\n            source_type=data_points[0].source_type,\n            analysis_period=(start_time, end_time),\n            data_points_analyzed=len(data_points),\n            quality_score=quality_score,\n            reliability_score=reliability_score,\n            uncertainty_score=uncertainty_score,\n            trends=trends,\n            recommendations=recommendations\n        )\n    \n    def _calculate_quality_score(self, data_points: List[HistoricalDataPoint]) -> DataQualityScore:\n        """Calculate overall quality score from data points."""\n        metric_scores: Dict[DataQualityMetric, List[float]] = defaultdict(list)\n        \n        # Collect all metric scores\n        for point in data_points:\n            for metric, score in point.quality_metrics.items():\n                metric_scores[metric].append(score)\n        \n        # Calculate average for each metric\n        avg_scores = {}\n        for metric in DataQualityMetric:\n            scores = metric_scores.get(metric, [])\n            avg_scores[metric] = statistics.mean(scores) if scores else 0.5\n        \n        return DataQualityScore(\n            completeness=avg_scores.get(DataQualityMetric.COMPLETENESS, 0.5),\n            accuracy=avg_scores.get(DataQualityMetric.ACCURACY, 0.5),\n            consistency=avg_scores.get(DataQualityMetric.CONSISTENCY, 0.5),\n            timeliness=avg_scores.get(DataQualityMetric.TIMELINESS, 0.5),\n            validity=avg_scores.get(DataQualityMetric.VALIDITY, 0.5),\n            uniqueness=avg_scores.get(DataQualityMetric.UNIQUENESS, 0.5),\n            overall=DataQualityScore.calculate_overall(avg_scores)\n        )\n    \n    def _calculate_reliability_score(self, data_points: List[HistoricalDataPoint]) -> float:\n        """\n        Calculate reliability score based on success/error rates.\n        \n        Returns:\n            Reliability score (0.0 to 1.0)\n        """\n        total_success = sum(p.success_count for p in data_points)\n        total_errors = sum(p.error_count for p in data_points)\n        total_operations = total_success + total_errors\n        \n        if total_operations == 0:\n            return 0.5  # Neutral score if no data\n        \n        success_rate = total_success / total_operations\n        \n        # Factor in consistency of success rate over time\n        if len(data_points) > 1:\n            success_rates = [\n                p.success_count / (p.success_count + p.error_count)\n                if (p.success_count + p.error_count) > 0 else 0.5\n                for p in data_points\n            ]\n            consistency = 1.0 - statistics.stdev(success_rates) if len(success_rates) > 1 else 1.0\n            \n            # Weighted average: 70% success rate, 30% consistency\n            return 0.7 * success_rate + 0.3 * consistency\n        \n        return success_rate\n    \n    def _analyze_trends(self, data_points: List[HistoricalDataPoint]) -> Dict[str, Any]:\n        """Analyze trends in the data."""\n        if len(data_points) < 2:\n            return {"trend": "insufficient_data"}\n        \n        # Sort by timestamp\n        sorted_points = sorted(data_points, key=lambda p: p.timestamp)\n        \n        # Calculate error rate trend\n        error_rates = [\n            p.error_count / (p.success_count + p.error_count)\n            if (p.success_count + p.error_count) > 0 else 0\n            for p in sorted_points\n        ]\n        \n        # Simple trend detection: compare first half to second half\n        mid = len(error_rates) // 2\n        first_half_avg = statistics.mean(error_rates[:mid]) if mid > 0 else 0\n        second_half_avg = statistics.mean(error_rates[mid:]) if mid > 0 else 0\n        \n        trend = "stable"\n        if second_half_avg > first_half_avg * 1.2:\n            trend = "degrading"\n        elif second_half_avg < first_half_avg * 0.8:\n            trend = "improving"\n        \n        return {\n            "trend": trend,\n            "error_rate_change": second_half_avg - first_half_avg,\n            "current_error_rate": error_rates[-1] if error_rates else 0,\n            "average_error_rate": statistics.mean(error_rates) if error_rates else 0\n        }\n    \n    def _generate_recommendations(\n        self,\n        quality_score: DataQualityScore,\n        reliability_score: float,\n        trends: Dict[str, Any]\n    ) -> List[str]:\n        """Generate recommendations based on analysis."""\n        recommendations = []\n        \n        # Quality-based recommendations\n        if quality_score.completeness < 0.7:\n            recommendations.append("Improve data completeness - missing fields detected")\n        \n        if quality_score.accuracy < 0.7:\n            recommendations.append("Verify data accuracy - inconsistencies detected")\n        \n        if quality_score.timeliness < 0.7:\n            recommendations.append("Update data more frequently - staleness detected")\n        \n        # Reliability-based recommendations\n        if reliability_score < 0.7:\n            recommendations.append("Investigate reliability issues - high error rate detected")\n        \n        if reliability_score < 0.5:\n            recommendations.append("CRITICAL: Consider alternative data source - reliability below threshold")\n        \n        # Trend-based recommendations\n        if trends.get("trend") == "degrading":\n            recommendations.append("WARNING: Data quality is degrading - immediate attention required")\n        \n        if trends.get("current_error_rate", 0) > 0.3:\n            recommendations.append("High current error rate - verify data source availability")\n        \n        return recommendations\n    \n    def _create_default_result(\n        self,\n        source_name: str,\n        start_time: datetime,\n        end_time: datetime\n    ) -> HistoricalAnalysisResult:\n        """Create default result when no data available."""\n        return HistoricalAnalysisResult(\n            source_name=source_name,\n            source_type=DataSourceType.EXTERNAL_SERVICE,\n            analysis_period=(start_time, end_time),\n            data_points_analyzed=0,\n            quality_score=DataQualityScore(\n                completeness=0.5,\n                accuracy=0.5,\n                consistency=0.5,\n                timeliness=0.5,\n                validity=0.5,\n                uniqueness=0.5,\n                overall=0.5\n            ),\n            reliability_score=0.5,\n            uncertainty_score=0.5,\n            trends={"trend": "no_data"},\n            recommendations=["No historical data available - cannot assess reliability"]\n        )\n    \n    def compare_sources(\n        self,\n        source_names: List[str],\n        analysis_period_hours: int = 168\n    ) -> Dict[str, HistoricalAnalysisResult]:\n        """\n        Compare multiple data sources.\n        \n        Args:\n            source_names: List of source names to compare\n            analysis_period_hours: Hours of history to analyze\n            \n        Returns:\n            Dictionary mapping source names to analysis results\n        """\n        results = {}\n        for source_name in source_names:\n            results[source_name] = self.analyze_source(source_name, analysis_period_hours)\n        return results\n    \n    def get_best_source(\n        self,\n        source_names: List[str],\n        analysis_period_hours: int = 168\n    ) -> Tuple[str, HistoricalAnalysisResult]:\n        """\n        Identify the best data source based on historical analysis.\n        \n        Args:\n            source_names: List of source names to compare\n            analysis_period_hours: Hours of        \n        if not results:\n            raise ValueError("No sources to compare")\n        \n        # Rank by reliability score\n        best_source = max(results.items(), key=lambda x: x[1].reliability_score)\n        return best_source\n\n\nclass UDCalculator:\n    """\n    Calculates UD (Uncertainty in Data) using historical analysis.\n    Integrates with Murphy\'s uncertainty analysis_period_hours: Hours of history to analyze\n            \n        Returns:\n            UD score (0.0 to 1.0, where 0 = certain, 1 = highly uncertain)\n        """\n        analysis = self.analyzer.analyze_source(source_name, analysis_period_hours)\n        \n        # UD is the uncertainty score from historical analysis\n        return analysis.uncertainty_score\n    \n    def calculate_ud_with_context(\n        self,\n        source_name: str,\n        context: Dict[str, Any]\n    ) -> Dict[str, Any]:\n        """\n        Calculate UD with additional context and       Dictionary with UD score and detailed breakdown\n        """\n        analysis_period = context.get("analysis_period_hours", 168)\n        analysis = self.analyzer.analyze_source(source_name, analysis_period)\n        \n        # Calculate component scores\n        quality_uncertainty = 1.0 - analysis.quality_score.overall\n        reliability_uncertainty = 1.0 - analysis.reliability_score\n        \n        # Weighted combination\n        ud_score = 0.6 * reliability_uncertainty + 0.4 * quality_uncertainty\n        \n        return {\n            "ud_score": HEALTHCARE = "healthcare"\n    FINANCE = "finance"\n    LEGAL = "legal"\n    ENGINEERING = "engineering"\n    EDUCATION = "education"\n    GENERAL = "general"\n\n\nclass AssumptionType(str, Enum):\n    """Types of assumptions."""\n    TECHNICAL = "technical"\n    BUSINESS_LOGIC = "business_logic"\n    USER_BEHAVIOR = "user_behavior"\n    DATA_QUALITY = "data_quality"\n    SYSTEM_BEHAVIOR = \n        Returns:\n            Dictionary with validation result and confidence\n        """\n        knowledge = self.get_domain_knowledge(domain)\n        if not knowledge:\n            return {\n      self.validation_history: Dict[str, List[AssumptionValidation]] = {}\n    \n    def calculate_expertise_score(self, expert: DomainExpert) -> ExpertiseScore:\n        """\n        Calculate certification_score = min(len(expert.certifications) / 5.0, 1.0)\n        \n        # Validation history score\n        validation_history_score = self._calculate_validation_history_score(expert.id)\n        \n        # Domain coverage score\n        domain_coverage_score = min(len(expert.domains) / 10.0, 1.0)\n        \n        # Verification bonus\n        verification_bonus = 0.1 if expert.verified else 0.0\n        \n        # Weighted overall score\n        overall_score = (\n            0.3 * experience_score +\n            0.2 * certification_score +\n            0.3 * validation_history_score +\n            0.2 * domain_coverage_score +\n            verification_bonus\n        )\n        \n        overall_score = min(overall_score, 1.0)\n        \n        return validation_history_score=validation_history_score,\n            domain_coverage_score=domain_coverage_score,\n            verification_status=expert.verified,\n            components={\n """Calculate score based on validation history."""\n        validations = self.validation_history.get(expert_id, [])\n        \n        if not validations:\n            return 0.5  # Neutral score for no history\n        \n        # Calculate accuracy of past validations\n        # In production, this would compare against actual outcomes\n        avg_confidence = statistics.mean([v.confidence for v in validations])\n        \n        # Factor in number of validations (more = better)\n        volume_factor = min(len(validations) / 50.0, 1.0)\n        \n        return 0.7 * avg_confidence + 0.3       expert_scores.append(expertise_score.overall_score)\n        \n        avg_expert_confidence = statistics.mean(expert_scores) if expert_scores else 0.5\n        \n        # Combine knowledge base and expert confidence\n        kb_confidence = kb_result.get("confidence", 0.5)\n        \n        # If knowledge base says invalid, increase uncertainty\n        if kb_result.get("is_valid") is      # Calculate UA\n        ua_score = self.calculate_ua(assumption, domain, assumption_type)\n        \n        return {\n            "ua_score": ua_score,\n            "assumption": assumption,\n "expert_details": expert_details,\n            "confidence_breakdown": {\n                "knowledge_base_confidence": kb_result.get("confidence", 0.5),\n                "expert_confidence": 1.0 -        source: InformationSource,\n        context: Dict[str, Any]\n    ) -> float:\n        """\n        Score source credibility with additional context.\n        \n        Context can include:\n        - author_verified: bool\n        - citations_count: int\n        - peer_reviews: int\n        - domain_authority: float\n        """\n        base_score = self.score_source(source)\n        \n        # Adjust based on context\n        if context.get("author_verified"):\n            base_score += 0.1\n        \n        citations = context.get("citations_count", 0)\n        if citations > 10:\n            base_score += 0.05\n        \n        peer_reviews = context.get("peer_reviews", 0)\n        if peer_reviews > 0:\n            base_score += 0.05\n        \n        domain_authority = content to assess quality metrics.\n    """\n    \n    def analyze_completeness(self, content: str, required_elements: Optional[List[str]] = None) -> float:\n        """\n        Analyze completeness of content.\n        \n        Args:\n            content: The content to analyze\n            required_elements: Optional list of required elements\n            \n        Returns:\n            Completeness score (0.0 to 1.0)\n        """\n        if not content:\n            return 0.0\n        \n        # Basic completeness checks\n        has_sufficient_length = len(content) > 100\n        has_structure = any(marker in content for marker in [\'\\n\\n\', \'. \', \'- \', \'* \'])\n        \n        score = 0.5\n        \n        if has_sufficient_length:\n            score += 0.25\n        \n        if has_structure:\n            score += 0.25\n        \n        # Check for required elements if provided\n        if required_elements:\n            found_elements = sum(1 for elem in required_elements if elem.lower() in content.lower())\n            element_score = found_elements / len(required_elements)\n            score = 0.5 * score + 0.5 * element_score\n        \n        return min(score, 1.0)\n    \n    def analyze_consistency(self, content: str) -> float:\n        """\n        Analyze internal consistency of content.\n        \n        Checks for contradictions, consistent terminology, etc.\n        """\n        if not content:\n            return 0.0\n        \n        # Simple consistency checks\n        sentences = content.split(\'. \')\n        \n        # Check for contradictory words\n        contradictions = [\'but\', \'however\', \'although\', \'despite\', \'nevertheless\']\n        contradiction_count = sum(1 for sent in sentences if any(word in sent.lower() for word in contradictions))\n        \n        # High contradiction ratio suggests inconsistency\n        if len(sentences) > 0:\n            contradiction_ratio = contradiction_count / len(sentences)\n            consistency_score = 1.0 - min(contradiction_ratio * 2, 1.0)\n        else:\n            consistency_score = 0.5\n        \n        return consistency_score\n    \n    def analyze_objectivity(self, content: str) -> float:\n        """\n        Analyze objectivity of content.\n        \n        Checks for subjective language, emotional words, etc.\n        """\n        if not content:\n            return 0.0\n        \n        # Subjective indicators\n        subjective_words = [\n            \'i think\', \'i believe\', \'in my opinion\', \'probably\', \'maybe\',\n            \'seems\', \'appears\', \'might\', \'could\', \'should\'\n        ]\n        \n        # Emotional words\n        emotional_words = [\n            \'amazing\', \'terrible\', \'awful\', \'fantastic\', \'horrible\',\n            \'love\', \'hate\', \'best\', \'worst\'\n        ]\n        \n        content_lower = content.lower()\n        \n        subjective_count = sum(1 for word in subjective_words if word in content_lower)\n        emotional_count = sum(1 for word in emotional_words if word in content_lower)\n        \n        total_indicators = subjective_count + emotional_count\n        \n        # Calculate objectivity (inverse of subjectivity)\n        word_count = len(content.split())\n        if word_count > 0:\n            subjectivity_ratio = total_indicators / (word_count / 100)  # per 100 words\n            objectivity_score = 1.0 - min(subjectivity_ratio, 1.0)\n        else:\n            objectivity_score = 0.5\n        \n        return objectivity_score\n    \n    def analyze_verifiability(self, content: str) -> float:\n        """\n        Analyze verifiability of content.\n        \n        Checks for citations, references, specific facts, etc.\n        """\n        if not content:\n            return 0.0\n        \n        score = 0.5\n        \n        # Check for URLs (citations)\n        url_pattern = r\'https?://[^\\s]+\'\n        urls = re.findall(url_pattern, content)\n        if urls:\n            score += 0.2\n        \n        # Check for specific numbers/dates (facts)\n        number_pattern = r\'\\b\\d+\\b\'\n        numbers = re.findall(number_pattern, content)\n        if len(numbers) > 3:\n            score += 0.15\n        \n        # Check for references section\n        if \'reference\' in content.lower() or \'citation\' in content.lower():\n            score += 0.15\n        \n        return min(score, 1.0)\n\n\nclass TimelinessAnalyzer:\n    """\n    Analyzes timeliness of information.\n    """\n    \n    def analyze_timeliness(\n        self,\n        published_date: Optional[datetime],\n        context: Dict[str, Any]\n    ) -> float:\n        """\n        Analyze timeliness of information.\n        \n        Args:\n            published_date: When the information was published\n            context: Additional context (e.g., topic_volatility)\n            \n        Returns:\n            Timeliness score (0.0 to 1.0)\n        """\n        if not published_date:\n            return 0.5  # Unknown date = neutral score\n        \n        age_days = (datetime.utcnow() - published_date).days\n        \n        # Get topic volatility (how quickly information becomes outdated)\n        # High volatility = information becomes outdated quickly\n        topic_volatility = context.get("topic_volatility", 0.5)\n        \n        # Calculate decay based on volatility\n        if topic_volatility > 0.8:  # High volatility (e.g., breaking news)\n            half_life_days = 7\n        elif topic_volatility > 0.5:  # Medium volatility (e.g., technology)\n            half_life_days = 90\n        else:  # Low volatility (e.g., historical facts)\n            half_life_days = 365\n        \n        # Exponential decay\n        timeliness = 2 ** (-age_days / half_life_days)\n        \n        return min(timeliness, 1.0)\n\n\nclass RelevanceAnalyzer:\n    """\n    Analyzes relevance of information to a query or context.\n    """\n    \n    def analyze_relevance(\n        self,\n        content: str,\n        query: str,\n        context: Dict[str, Any]\n    ) -> float:\n        """\n        Analyze relevance of content to a query.\n        \n        Args:\n            content: The content to analyze\n            query: The query or topic\n            context: Additional context\n            \n        Returns:\n            Relevance score (0.0 to 1.0)\n        """\n        if not content or not query:\n            return 0.0\n        \n        content_lower = content.lower()\n        query_lower = query.lower()\n        \n        # Extract keywords from query\n        query_words = set(query_lower.split())\n        \n        # Count keyword matches\n        matches = sum(1 for word in query_words if word in content_lower)\n        \n        if len(query_words) > 0:\n            keyword_score = matches / len(query_words)\n        else:\n            keyword_score = 0.0\n        \n        # Check for exact phrase match\n        phrase_match = query_lower in content_lower\n        \n        # Calculate relevance\n        relevance = 0.7 * keyword_score\n        if phrase_match:\n            relevance += 0.3\n        \n        return min(relevance, 1.0)\n\n\nclass InformationQualityAnalyzer:\n    """\n    Main analyzer that coordinates all quality assessments.\n    """\n    \n    def __init__(self):\n        self.credibility_scorer = SourceCredibilityScorer()\n        self.content_analyzer = ContentAnalyzer()\n        self.timeliness_analyzer = TimelinessAnalyzer()\n        self.relevance_analyzer = RelevanceAnalyzer()\n    \n    def assess_information(\n        self,\n        information: InformationItem,\n        context: Optional[Dict[str, Any]] = None\n    ) -> InformationQualityAssessment:\n        """\n        Perform comprehensive quality assessment.\n        \n        Args:\n            information: The information to assess\n            context: Additional context for assessment\n            \n        Returns:\n            InformationQualityAssessment with detailed metrics\n        """\n        context = context or {}\n        \n        # Assess each dimension\n        metrics = InformationMetrics()\n        \n        # Credibility (based on source)\n        metrics.credibility = self.credibility_scorer.score_source_with_context(\n            information.source,\n            context\n        )\n        \n        # Content-based metrics\n        metrics.completeness = self.content_analyzer.analyze_completeness(\n            information.content,\n            context.get("required_elements")\n        )\n        \n        metrics.consistency = self.content_analyzer.analyze_consistency(\n            information.content\n        )\n        \n        metrics.objectivity = self.content_analyzer.analyze_objectivity(\n            information.content\n        )\n        \n        metrics.verifiability = self.content_analyzer.analyze_verifiability(\n            information.content\n        )\n        \n        # Timeliness\n        metrics.timeliness = self.timeliness_analyzer.analyze_timeliness(\n            information.published_date,\n            context\n        )\n        \n        # Relevance\n        query = context.get("query", "")\n        metrics.relevance = self.relevance_analyzer.analyze_relevance(\n            information.content,\n            query,\n            context\n        )\n        \n        # Accuracy (requires external validation, default to credibility)\n        metrics.accuracy = metrics.credibility\n        \n        # Calculate overall quality\n        metrics.overall_quality = metrics.calculate_overall()\n        \n        # Identify issues\n        issues = self._identify_issues(metrics)\n        \n        # Generate recommendations\n        recommendations = self._generate_recommendations(metrics, issues)\n        \n        # Calculate uncertainty (inverse of quality)\n        uncertainty_score = 1.0 - metrics.overall_quality\n        \n        return InformationQualityAssessment(\n            information_id=information.id,\n            metrics=metrics,\n            quality_score=metrics.overall_quality,\n            uncertainty_score=uncertainty_score,\n            issues=issues,\n            recommendations=recommendations\n        )\n    \n    def _identify_issues(self, metrics: InformationMetrics) -> List[str]:\n        """Identify quality issues based on metrics."""\n        issues = []\n        \n        threshold = 0.6\n        \n        if metrics.accuracy < threshold:\n            issues.append("Low accuracy score - verify information")\n        \n        if metrics.completeness < threshold:\n            issues.append("Incomplete information - missing key elements")\n        \n        if metrics.consistency < threshold:\n            issues.append("Internal inconsistencies detected")\n        \n        if metrics.timeliness < threshold:\n            issues.append("Information may be outdated")\n        \n        if metrics.relevance < threshold:\n            issues.append("Low relevance to query")\n        \n        if metrics.credibility < threshold:\n            issues.append("Low source credibility")\n        \n        if metrics.objectivity < threshold:\n            issues.append("Subjective or biased content")\n        \n        if metrics.verifiability < threshold:\n            issues.append("Difficult to verify - lacks citations")\n        \n        return issues\n    \n    def _generate_recommendations(\n        self,\n        metrics: InformationMetrics,\n        issues: List[str]\n    ) -> List[str]:\n        """Generate recommendations based on issues."""\n        recommendations = []\n        \n        if metrics.credibility < 0.6:\n            recommendations.append("Seek additional sources with higher credibility")\n        \n        if metrics.completeness < 0.6:\n            recommendations.append("Gather additional information to fill gaps")\n        \n        if metrics.timeliness < 0.6:\n            recommendations.append("Look for more recent information")\n        \n        if metrics.verifiability < 0.6:\n            recommendations.append("Cross-reference with verifiable sources")\n        \n        if metrics.overall_quality < 0.5:\n            recommendations.append("CRITICAL: Information quality is poor - use with caution")\n        \n        return recommendations\n\n\nclass UICalculator:\n    """\n    Calculates UI (Uncertainty in Information) using quality metrics.\n    Integrates with information: The information to assess\n            context: Additional context\n            \n        Returns:\n            UI score (0.0 to 1.0, where 0 = certain, 1 = highly uncertain)\n        """\n        assessment = self.analyzer.assess_information(information, context)\n        return assessment.uncertainty_score\n    \n    def calculate_ui_detailed(\n        self,\n        information: information: The information to assess\n            context: Additional context\n            \n        Returns:\n            Dictionary with UI score and detailed breakdown\n        """\n        assessment = self.analyzer.assess_information(information, context)\n        \n        return {\n            "ui_score": assessment.uncertainty_score,\n            "quality_score": assessment.quality_score,\n            "metrics": {\n                "accuracy": assessment.metrics.accuracy,\n                "completeness": assessment.metrics.completeness,\n                "consistency": assessment.metrics.consistency,\n                "timeliness": assessment.metrics.timeliness,\n                "relevance": assessment.metrics.relevance,\n                "credibility": assessment.metrics.credibility,\n                "objectivity": assessment.metrics.objectivity,\n                "verifiability": assessment.metrics.verifiability\n            },\n            "issues": assessment.issues,\n            "recommendations": assessment.recommendations,\n            "source": information.source,\n            "age_days": information.age_in_days()\n        }\n\n\nclass InformationQualitySystem:\n    """\n    Complete information quality metrics system.\n    Provides unified interface for quality assessment and UI calculation.\n    """\n    \n    def availability_pct > 50:\n                resource.status = ResourceStatus.LIMITED\n            elif availability_pct > 20:\n                resource.status = ResourceStatus.DEGRADED\n            else:\n                resource.status = ResourceStatus.UNAVAILABLE\n        \n        # Record usage history\n        utilization = resource.utilization_percentage()\n """Get usage trend for a resource."""\n        history = self.usage_history.get(resource_id, [])\n        if not history:\n            return {"trend": "unknown", "average_utilization": 0.0}\n        \n        cutoff = datetime.utcnow() - timedelta(hours=hours)\n        recent_history = [(ts, util) for ts, util in history if ts >= cutoff]\n        \n        if not recent_history:\n \n        # Determine trend\n        if len(utilizations) > 1:\n            mid = len(utilizations) // 2\n            first_half_avg = sum(utilizations[:mid]) / mid\n            second_half_avg = if utilizations else 0.0\n        }\n\n\nclass ResourceAvailabilityChecker:\n    """\n    Checks resource availability against requirements.\n    """\n    \n    def __init__(self, monitor: ResourceStatus.UNAVAILABLE:\n            issues.append("Resource is unavailable")\n            recommendations.append("Wait for resource to become available or use alternative")\n        \n        # Check usage trend\n        trend = self.monitor.get_usage_trend(resource_id)\n        if trend["trend"] == "increasing" and trend["average_utilization"] > 70:\n            issues.append("Resource         resource_type=resource.resource_type,\n            is_available=is_available,\n            available_amount=resource.available_capacity,\n            required_amount=required_amount,\n            sufficiency_score=sufficiency_score,\n            status=resource.status,\n            issues=issues,\n            recommendations=recommendations\n        )\n    \n    async def check_multiple_resources(\n        self,\n        requirements: List[Tuple[str, float]]\n    ) -> List[ResourceAvailabilityCheck]:\n        """\n        Check multiple resources in parallel.\n        \n        Args:\n            requirements: List of (resource_id, required_amount) tuples\n            \n        Returns:\n            List of ResourceAvailabilityCheck results\n        """\n        tasks = [\n            self.check_resource_availability(resource_id, amount)\n            for resource_id, amount in requirements\n        ]\n        return await asyncio.gather(*tasks)\n    \n    def check_resource_by_type(\n        self,\n        resource_type: ResourceType,\n        required_amount: float\n    ) -> Optional[ResourceAvailabilityCheck]:\n        """\n        Check availability for any resource of a given type.\n        \n        Args:\n            resource_type: Type of resource needed\n            required_amount: Amount required\n            \n        Returns:\n            ResourceAvailabilityCheck for best available resource, or None\n        """\n        resources = self.monitor.get_resources_by_type(resource_type)\n        \n        if not resources:\n            return None\n        \n        # Find resource with most available capacity\n        best_resource = max(resources, key=lambda r: r.available_capacity)\n        \n        # Use asyncio.run for synchronous context\n        return asyncio.run(\n            self.check_resource_availability(best_resource.id, required_amount)\n        )\n\n\nclass ResourceAllocator:\n    """\n    Allocates create_allocation_plan(\n        self,\n        requirements: List[ResourceRequirement]\n    ) -> ResourceAllocationPlan:\n        """\n        Create a resource allocation plan.\n        \n        Args:\n            requirements: List of resource requirements\n            \n        Returns:\n            ResourceAllocationPlan with allocations and feasibility\n        """\n        plan_id = f"plan_{datetime.utcnow().timestamp()}"\n        allocations = {}\n        feasible = True\n        confidence_scores = []\n        constraints = []\n        estimated_cost = 0.0\n        \n        for req in requirements:\n            # Find available resource of this type\n            check = self.checker.check_resource_by_type(\n                req.resource_type,\n                req.required_amount\n            )\n            \n            if not check:\n                feasible = False\n                constraints.append(f"No {req.resource_type} resources registered")\n                confidence_scores.append(0.0)\n                continue\n            \n            if not check.is_available:\n                if req.priority >= 4:  # Critical priority\n                    feasible = False\n                constraints.append(f"Insufficient {req.resource_type}")\n            \n            allocations[check.resource_id] = req.required_amount\n            confidence_scores.append(check.sufficiency_score)\n            \n            # Estimate cost (placeholder - would use actual pricing)\n            if req.resource_type == ResourceType.COMPUTE:\n                estimated_cost += req.required_amount * 0.10  # $0.10 per core-hour\n            elif req.resource_type == ResourceType.STORAGE:\n                estimated_cost += req.required_amount * 0.02  # $0.02 per GB\n        \n        # Calculate overall confidence\n        overall_confidence = sum(confidence_scores) / len(confidence_scores) if confidence_scores else 0.0\n        \n        return ResourceAllocationPlan(\n            plan_id=plan_id,\n            requirements=requirements,\n            allocations=allocations,\n            feasible=feasible,\n            confidence=overall_confidence,\n            estimated_cost=estimated_cost,\n            constraints=constraints\n        )\n\n\nclass URCalculator:\n    """\n    Calculates UR (Uncertainty in Resources) using availability checks.\n    Integrates with Murphy\'s uncertainty framework.\n    """\n    \n    def __init__(self, allocator: ResourceAllocator):\n        self.allocator = allocator\n    \n    async def calculate_ur(\n        self,\n        requirements: List[ResourceRequirement]\n    ) -> float:\n        """\n        Calculate UR score for resource requirements.\n        \n        Args:\n            requirements: List of resource requirements\n            \n        Returns:\n            UR score (0.0 to 1.0, where 0 = certain, 1 = highly uncertain)\n        """\n        plan = await self.allocator.create_allocation_plan(requirements)\n        \n        # UR is inverse of confidence\n        ur_score = 1.0 - plan.confidence\n        \n        # Increase uncertainty if not feasible\n        if not plan.feasible:\n            ur_score = max(ur_score, 0.8)\n        \n        return ur_score\n    \n    async def calculate_ur_detailed(\n        self,\n        requirements: List[ResourceRequirement],\n        context: Optional[Dict[str, Any]] = None\n    ) -> Dict[str, Any]:\n        """\n        Calculate UR with detailed breakdown.\n        \n        Args:\n            requirements: List of resource requirements\n            context: Additional context\n            \n        Returns:\n            Dictionary with UR score and detailed breakdown\n        """\n        plan = await self.allocator.create_allocation_plan(requirements)\n        ur_score = 1.0 - plan.confidence\n        \n        if not plan.feasible:\n            ur_score = max(ur_score, 0.8)\n        \n        return {\n            "ur_score": ur_score,\n            "confidence": plan.confidence,\n            "feasible": plan.feasible,\n            "allocations": plan.allocations,\n            "constraints": plan.constraints,\n            "estimated_cost": plan.estimated_cost,\n            "requirements_count": len(requirements),\n            "critical_requirements": sum(1 for r in requirements if r.priority >= 4)\n        }\n\n\nclass ResourceAvailabilitySystem:\n    """\n    Complete resource availability checking system.\n    Provides unified interface for resource monitoring and UR calculation.\n    """\n    \n    def __init__(self):\n        self.monitor = ResourceMonitor()\n        self.checker = ResourceAvailabilityChecker(self.monitor)\n        self.allocator = ResourceAllocator(self.checker)\n        self.ur_calculator = URCalculator(self.allocator)\n    \n    def register_resource(\n        self,\n        name: str,\n        resource_type: ResourceType,\n        total_capacity: float,\n        available_capacity: float,\n        unit: ResourceUnit,\n        metadata: Optional[Dict[str, Any]] = None\n    ) -> str:\n        """Register a new resource."""\n        resource = Resource(\n            id=f"{resource_type}_{datetime.utcnow().timestamp()}",\n            name=name,\n            resource_type=resource_type,\n            total_capacity=total_capacity,\n            available_capacity=available_capacity,\n            unit=unit,\n            metadata=metadata or {}\n        )\n        return self.monitor.register_resource(resource)\n    \n    def update_resource(\n        self,\n        resource_id: str,\n        available_capacity: float,\n        status: Optional[ResourceStatus] = None\n    ):\n        """Update resource availability."""\n        self.monitor.update_resource(resource_id, available_capacity, status)\n    \n    async def check_availability(\n        self,\n        resource_id: str,\n        required_amount: float\n    ) -> ResourceAvailabilityCheck:\n        """Check resource availability."""\n        return await self.checker.check_resource_availability(resource_id, required_amount)\n    \n    async def calculate_ur(\n        self,\n        requirements: List[ResourceRequirement]\n    ) -> float:\n        """Calculate UR score."""\n        return await self.ur_calculator.calculate_ur(requirements)\n    \n    async def calculate_ur_detailed(\n        self,\n        requirements: List[ResourceRequirement],\n        context: Optional[Dict[str, Any]] = None\n    ) -> Dict[str, Any]:\n        """Calculate UR with detailed breakdown."""\n        return await self.ur_calculator.calculate_ur_detailed(requirements, context)\n    \n    def get_resource_status(self, resource_id: str) -> Optional[Dict[str, Any]]:\n        """Get current status of a resource."""\n        resource = self.monitor.get_resource(resource_id)\n        if not resource:\n            return None\n        \n        trend = self.monitor.get_usage_trend(resource_id)\n        \n        return {\n            "resource_id": resource.id,\n            "name": resource.name,\n            "type": resource.resource_type,\n            "status": resource.status,\n            "total_capacity": resource.total_capacity,\n            "available_capacity": resource.available_capacity,\n            "utilization_percentage": resource.utilization_percentage(),\n            "availability_percentage": resource.availability_percentage(),\n            "unit": resource.unit,\n            "last_checked": resource.last_checked.isoformat(),\n            "usage_trend": trend\n \n    def add_risk_pattern(self, pattern: RiskPattern) -> str:\n        """Add a risk pattern to the database."""\n        self.risk_patterns[pattern.id] = pattern\n        \n        # Update     patterns = [p for p in patterns if p.id in matching_ids]\n        \n        if min_risk_score is not None:\n            patterns = [p for p in patterns if p.risk_score >= min_risk_score]\n        \n        return patterns\n    \n    def add_risk_incident(self, incident: RiskIncident) -> str:\n        """Record a risk incident."""\n        self.risk_incidents[incident.id] = incident\n        \n        # Update pattern occurrence count\n        pattern = self.risk_patterns.get(incident.risk_pattern_id)\n        if pattern:\n            pattern.occurrence_count += 1\n            pattern.last_occurred = incident.occurred_at\n        \n        return incident.id\n    \n    def get_risk_incidents(\n        self,\n        pattern_id: Optional[str] = None,\n        status: breakdown\n        category_counts = {}\n        for category in RiskCategory:\n            category_counts[category.value] = len(self.category_index.get(category, []))\n        \n        # Severity breakdown\n        severity_counts = {}\n        for severity in RiskSeverity:\n            severity_counts[severity.value] = len(self.severity_index.get(severity, []))\n        \n        # Average risk score\n        risk_scores = [p.risk_score for p in self.risk_patterns.values()]\n        avg_risk_score = sum(risk_scores) / len(risk_scores) if risk_scores else 0.0\n        \n        return {\n            "total_patterns": total_patterns,\n            "total_incidents": total_incidents,\n            "category_breakdown": category_counts,\n            "severity_breakdown":  "risk_patterns": [p.dict() for p in self.risk_patterns.values()],\n            "risk_incidents": [i.dict() for i in self.risk_incidents.values()],\n            "mitigation_strategies": [s.dict() for   json.dump(data, f, indent=2, default=str)\n    \n    def import_from_json(self, filepath: str):\n        """Import database from JSON file."""\n        with open(filepath, \'r\') as f:\n            data = json.load(f)\n        \n        for pattern_data in data.get("risk_patterns", []):\n            pattern = RiskPattern(**pattern_data)\n            self.add_risk_pattern(pattern)\n        \n {'role': 'assistant', 'content': '## Task 2.2: Implementing Risk Pattern Storage\n\nNow I\'ll create a comprehensive risk pattern storage system with advanced querying capabilities.\n\n<function_calls>\n<create-file file_path="murphy_implementation/risk/risk_storage.py">\n"""\nRisk Pattern Storage System\nAdvanced storage and retrieval for risk patterns with pattern matching.\n"""\n\nfrom typing import Dict, List, Optional, Any, Tuple\nfrom datetime import datetime, timedelta\nfrom enum import Enum\nfrom pydantic import BaseModel, Field\nimport re\nfrom collections import defaultdict\n\nfrom murphy_implementation.risk.risk_database import (\n    RiskPattern, RiskCategory, RiskSeverity, RiskLikelihood,\n    RiskIncident, MitigationStrategy, RiskDatabase\n)\n\n\nclass PatternMatchType(str, Enum):\n    """Types of pattern matching."""\n    EXACT = "exact"\n    KEYWORD = "keyword"\n    FUZZY = "fuzzy"\n    CONTEXT = "context"\n    SEMANTIC = "semantic"\n\n\nclass PatternMatchResult(BaseModel):\n    """Result of pattern matching."""\n    pattern_id: str\n    pattern_name: str\n    match_score: float = Field(ge=0.0, le=1.0)\n    match_type: PatternMatchType\n    matched_keywords: List[str] = Field(default_factory=list)\n    matched_contexts: List[str] = Field(default_factory=list)\n    confidence: float = Field(ge=0.0, le=1.0)\n\n\nclass RiskPatternQuery(BaseModel):\n    """Query for searching risk patterns."""\n    text: Optional[str] = None\n    category: Optional[RiskCategory] = None\n    severity: Optional[RiskSeverity] = None\n    min_risk_score: Optional[float] = None\n    max_risk_score: Optional[float] = None\n    tags: Optional[List[str]] = None\n    keywords: Optional[List[str]] = None\n    match_type: PatternMatchType = PatternMatchType.KEYWORD\n    limit: int = 10\n\n\nclass RiskPatternMatcher:\n    """\n    Matches text against risk patterns using various algorithms.\n    """\n    \n    def __init__(self, database: RiskDatabase):\n        self.database = database\n    \n    def match_patterns(\n        self,\n        text: str,\n        match_type: PatternMatchType = PatternMatchType.KEYWORD,\n        min_score: float = 0.3\n    ) -> List[PatternMatchResult]:\n        """\n        Match text against all risk patterns.\n        \n        Args:\n            text: Text to match against patterns\n            match_type: Type of matching to perform\n            min_score: Minimum match score threshold\n            \n        Returns:\n            List of PatternMatchResult sorted by score\n        """\n        results = []\n        text_lower = text.lower()\n        \n        for pattern in self.database.risk_patterns.values():\n            if match_type == PatternMatchType.EXACT:\n                score = self._exact_match(text_lower, pattern)\n            elif match_type == PatternMatchType.KEYWORD:\n                score = self._keyword_match(text_lower, pattern)\n            elif match_type == PatternMatchType.CONTEXT:\n                score = self._context_match(text_lower, pattern)\n            elif match_type == PatternMatchType.FUZZY:\n                score = self._fuzzy_match(text_lower, pattern)\n            else:\n                score = self._keyword_match(text_lower, pattern)\n            \n            if score >= min_score:\n                matched_keywords = [\n                    kw for kw in pattern.keywords\n                    if kw.lower() in text_lower\n                ]\n                \n                matched_contexts = [\n                    ctx for ctx in pattern.context_patterns\n                    if ctx.lower() in text_lower\n                ]\n                \n                results.append(PatternMatchResult(\n                    pattern_id=pattern.id,\n                    pattern_name=pattern.name,\n                    match_score=score,\n                    match_type=match_type,\n                    matched_keywords=matched_keywords,\n                    matched_contexts=matched_contexts,\n                    confidence=score\n                ))\n        \n        # Sort by match score\n        results.sort(key=lambda r: r.match_score, reverse=True)\n        return results\n    \n    def _exact_match(self, text: str, pattern: RiskPattern) -> float:\n        """Exact string matching."""\n        if pattern.name.lower() in text:\n            return 1.0\n        if pattern.description.lower() in text:\n            return 0.8\n        return 0.0\n    \n    def _keyword_match(self, text: str, pattern: RiskPattern) -> float:\n        """Keyword-based matching."""\n        if not pattern.keywords:\n            return 0.0\n        \n        matched_keywords = sum(1 for kw in pattern.keywords if kw.lower() in text)\n        score = matched_keywords / len(pattern.keywords)\n        \n        return score\n    \n    def _context_match(self, text: str, pattern: RiskPattern) -> float:\n        """Context pattern matching."""\n        keyword_score = self._keyword_match(text, pattern)\n        \n        if not pattern.context_patterns:\n            return keyword_score\n        \n        matched_contexts = sum(1 for ctx in pattern.context_patterns if ctx.lower() in text)\n        context_score = matched_contexts / len(pattern.context_patterns)\n        \n        # Weighted combination\n        return 0.6 * keyword_score + 0.4 * context_score\n    \n    def _fuzzy_match(self, text: str, pattern: RiskPattern) -> float:\n        """Fuzzy matching with partial word matches."""\n        score = 0.0\n        text_words = set(text.split())\n        \n        # Check keywords with fuzzy matching\n        for keyword in pattern.keywords:\n            keyword_words = set(keyword.lower().split())\n            \n            # Calculate word overlap\n            overlap = len(text_words & keyword_words)\n            if overlap > 0:\n                score += overlap / len(keyword_words)\n        \n        if pattern.keywords:\n            score = score / len(pattern.keywords)\n        \n        return min(score, 1.0)\n\n\nclass RiskPatternStorage:\n    """\n    Advanced storage system for risk patterns with indexing and caching.\n    """\n    \n    def __init__(self, database: RiskDatabase):\n        self.database = database\n        self.matcher = RiskPatternMatcher(database)\n        self.query_cache: Dict[str, Tuple[datetime, List[PatternMatchResult]]] = {}\n        self.cache_ttl_seconds = 300  # 5 minutes\n    \n    def store_pattern(\n        self,\n        name: str,\n        description: str,\n        category: RiskCategory,\n        severity: RiskSeverity,\n        likelihood: RiskLikelihood,\n        impact_score: float,\n        keywords: List[str],\n        context_patterns: Optional[List[str]] = None,\n        mitigation_strategies: Optional[List[MitigationStrategy]] = None,\n        tags: Optional[List[str]] = None,\n        metadata: Optional[Dict[str, Any]] = None\n    ) -> str:\n        """\n        Store a new risk pattern.\n        \n        Args:\n            name: Name of the risk pattern\n            description: Detailed description\n            category: Risk category\n            severity: Severity level\n            likelihood: Likelihood of occurrence\n            impact_score: Impact score (0-10)\n            keywords: Keywords for pattern matching\n            context_patterns: Context patterns for matching\n            mitigation_strategies: List of mitigation strategies\n            tags: Tags for categorization\n            metadata: Additional metadata\n            \n        Returns:\n            Pattern ID\n        """\n        # Calculate probability from likelihood\n        likelihood_map = {\n            RiskLikelihood.VERY_HIGH: 0.9,\n            RiskLikelihood.HIGH: 0.7,\n            RiskLikelihood.MEDIUM: 0.5,\n            RiskLikelihood.LOW: 0.3,\n            RiskLikelihood.VERY_LOW: 0.1\n        }\n        probability_score = likelihood_map.get(likelihood, 0.5)\n        \n        pattern = RiskPattern(\n            id=f"risk_{datetime.utcnow().timestamp()}",\n            name=name,\n            description=description,\n            category=category,\n            severity=severity,\n            likelihood=likelihood,\n            impact_score=impact_score,\n            probability_score=probability_score,\n            risk_score=impact_score * probability_score,\n            keywords=set(keywords),\n            context_patterns=context_patterns or [],\n            mitigation_strategies=mitigation_strategies or [],\n            tags=tags or [],\n            metadata=metadata or {}\n        )\n        \n        return self.database.add_risk_pattern(pattern)\n    \n    def get_pattern(self, pattern_id: str) -> Optional[RiskPattern]:\n        """Retrieve a risk pattern by ID."""\n        return self.database.get_risk_pattern(pattern_id)\n    \n    def update_pattern(\n        self,\n        pattern_id: str,\n        updates: Dict[str, Any]\n    ) -> bool:\n        """\n        Update a risk pattern.\n        \n        Args:\n            pattern_id: ID of pattern to update\n            updates: Dictionary of fields to update\n            \n        Returns:\n            True if successful, False otherwise\n        """\n        pattern = self.database.get_risk_pattern(pattern_id)\n        if not pattern:\n            return False\n        \n        # Update fields\n        for key, value in updates.items():\n            if hasattr(pattern, key):\n                setattr(pattern, key, value)\n        \n        # Recalculate risk score if impact or probability changed\n        if \'impact_score\' in updates or \'probability_score\' in updates:\n            pattern.risk_score = pattern.calculate_risk_score()\n        \n        pattern.updated_at = datetime.utcnow()\n        \n        # Clear cache\n        self.query_cache.clear()\n        \n        return True\n    \n    def delete_pattern(self, pattern_id: str) -> bool:\n        """Delete a risk pattern."""\n        if pattern_id in self.database.risk_patterns:\n            del self.database.risk_patterns[pattern_id]\n            self.query_cache.clear()\n            return True\n        return False\n    \n    def search_patterns(self, query: RiskPatternQuery) -> List[RiskPattern]:\n        """\n        Search for risk patterns using a query.\n        \n        Args:\n            query: RiskPatternQuery with search criteria\n            \n        Returns:\n            List of matching RiskPattern objects\n        """\n        # Check cache\n        cache_key = self._get_cache_key(query)\n        if cache_key in self.query_cache:\n            cached_time, cached_results = self.query_cache[cache_key]\n            if (datetime.utcnow() - cached_time).seconds < self.cache_ttl_seconds:\n                # Return cached patterns\n                return [\n                    self.database.get_risk_pattern(r.pattern_id)\n                    for r in cached_results[:query.limit]\n                    if self.database.get_risk_pattern(r.pattern_id)\n                ]\n        \n        # Perform search\n        patterns = min_risk_score=query.min_risk_score\n        )\n        \n        # Apply max risk score filter\n        if query.max_risk_score is not None:\n            patterns = [p for p in patterns if p.risk_score <= query.max_risk_score]\n        \n        # Apply text matching if provided\n        if query.text:\n            match_results = self.matcher.match_patterns(\n                query.text,\n                query.match_type\n            )\n            \n            # Cache results\n            self.query_cache[cache_key] = (datetime.utcnow(), match_results)\n            \n            # Filter patterns by match results\n            matched_ids = {r.pattern_id for r in match_results}\n            patterns = [p for p in patterns if p.id in matched_ids]\n            \n            # Sort by match score\n            pattern_scores = {r.pattern_id: r.match_score for r in match_results}\n            patterns.sort(key=lambda p: pattern_scores.get(p.id, 0), reverse=True)\n        \n        return patterns[:query.limit]\n    \n    def find_similar_patterns(\n        self,\n        pattern_id: str,\n        limit: int = 5\n    ) -> List[Tuple[RiskPattern, float]]:\n        """\n        Find patterns similar to a given pattern.\n        \n        Args:\n            pattern_id: ID of the reference pattern\n            limit: Maximum number of similar patterns to return\n            \n        Returns:\n            List of (pattern, similarity_score) tuples\n        """\n        reference = self.database.get_risk_pattern(pattern_id)\n        if not reference:\n            return []\n        \n        similar = []\n        \n        for pattern in self.database.risk_patterns.values():\n            if pattern.id == pattern_id:\n                continue\n            \n            similarity = self._calculate_similarity(reference, pattern)\n            if similarity > 0.3:  # Threshold\n                similar.append((pattern, similarity))\n        \n        # Sort by similarity\n        similar.sort(key=lambda x: x[1], reverse=True)\n        return similar[:limit]\n    \n    def _calculate_similarity(\n        self,\n        pattern1: RiskPattern,\n        pattern2: RiskPattern\n    ) -> float:\n        """Calculate similarity between two patterns."""\n        score = 0.0\n        \n        # Category match\n        if pattern1.category == pattern2.category:\n            score += 0.3\n        \n        # Severity match\n        if pattern1.severity == pattern2.severity:\n            score += 0.2\n        \n        # Keyword overlap\n        if pattern1.keywords and pattern2.keywords:\n            overlap = len(pattern1.keywords & pattern2.keywords)\n            total = len(pattern1.keywords | pattern2.keywords)\n            if total > 0:\n                score += 0.3 * (overlap / total)\n        \n        # Risk score similarity\n        if pattern1.risk_score > 0 and pattern2.risk_score > 0:\n            score_diff = abs(pattern1.risk_score - pattern2.risk_score)\n            score += 0.2 * (1 - min(score_diff / 10.0, 1.0))\n        \n        return score\n    \n    def _get_cache_key(self, query: RiskPatternQuery) -> str:\n        """Generate cache key for a query."""\n        return f"{query.text}_{query.category}_{query.severity}_{query.match_type}"\n    \n    def get_patterns_by_risk_level(\n        self,\n        min_score: float = 0.0,\n        max_score: float = 10.0\n    ) -> Dict[str, List[RiskPattern]]:\n        """\n        Get patterns grouped by risk level.\n        \n        Args:\n            min_score: Minimum risk score\n            max_score: Maximum risk score\n            \n        Returns:\n            Dictionary with risk levels as keys \n        grouped = {\n            "critical": [],  # 8-10\n            "high": [],      # 6-8\n            "medium": [],    # 4-6\n            "low": [],       # 2-4\n            "negligible": [] # 0-2\n        }\n        \n        for pattern in patterns:\n            if pattern.risk_score >= 8:\n                grouped["critical"].append(pattern)\n            elif pattern.risk_score >= 6:\n                grouped["high"].append(pattern)\n            elif pattern.risk_score >= 4:\n                grouped["medium"].append(pattern)\n            elif pattern.risk_score >= 2:\n                grouped["low"].append(pattern)\n            else:\n                grouped["negligible"].append(pattern)\n        \n        return grouped\n    \n    def get_trending_risks(\n        self,\n        days: int = 30,\n        limit: int = 10\n    ) -> List[Tuple[RiskPattern, int]]:\n        """\n        Get trending risks based on recent incidents.\n        \n        Args:\n            days: Number of days to look back\n            limit: Maximum number of risks to return\n            \n        Returns:\n            List of (pattern, incident_count) tuples\n        """\n        cutoff =           if incident.occurred_at >= cutoff:\n                incident_counts[incident.risk_pattern_id] += 1\n        \n        # Get patterns with counts\n        trending = []\n        for pattern_id, count in incident_counts.items():\n            pattern = self.database.get_risk_pattern(pattern_id)\n            if pattern:\n                trending.append((pattern, count))\n        \n        # Sort by count\n        trending.sort(key=lambda x: x[1], reverse=True)\n        return trending[:limit]\n    \n    def export_patterns(\n        self,\n        category: Optional[RiskCategory] = None,\n        severity: Optional[RiskSeverity] = None\n    ) -> List[Dict[str, Any]]:\n        """\n        Export patterns as dictionaries.\n        \n        Args:\n            category: Optional dictionaries\n            \n        Returns:\n            List of imported pattern IDs\n        """\n        imported_ids = []\n        \n        for data in patterns_data:\n            try:\n                pattern = RiskPattern(**data)\n                pattern_id = self.database.add_risk_pattern(pattern)\n                imported_ids.append(pattern_id)\n            except Exception as e:\n                print(f"Error importing pattern: {e}")\n                continue\n        \n        return imported_ids\n    \n    def get_storage_statistics(self) -> Dict[str, Any]:\n        """Get threshold\n            \n        Returns:\n            RiskIdentificationResult with identified risks\n        """\n        # Check cache\n        cache_key = self.cache.get_cache_key(text, context)\n        cached_result = self.cache.get(cache_key)\n        if cached_result:\n            return cached_result\n        \n        # Perform pattern matching\n        match_results = self.storage.matcher.match_patterns(\n            text,\n            match_type=PatternMatchType.CONTEXT,\n            min_score=min_match_score\n        )\n        \n        if not match_results:\n            result = RiskIdentificationResult(\n                identified_risks=[],\n                total_risk_score=0.0,\n                confidence=1.0\n            )\n            self.cache.set(cache_key, result)\n            return result\n        \n        # Get full pattern details\n        patterns = []\n        for match in match_results:\n            pattern = self.storage.get_pattern(match.pattern_id)\n            if pattern:\n                patterns.append((match, pattern))\n        \n        # Calculate total risk score (weighted by match confidence)\n        total_risk_score = sum(\n            pattern.risk_score * match.match_score\n            for match, pattern in patterns\n        )\n        \n        # Normalize to 0-10 scale\n        if patterns:\n            total_risk_score = min(total_risk_score / len(patterns), 10.0)\n        \n        # Find highest severity\n        highest_severity = None\n        if patterns:\n            highest_severity = max(\n                (pattern.severity for _, pattern in patterns),\n                key=lambda s: self.severity_order.get(s, 0)\n            )\n        \n        # Count by severity\n        severity_counts = {}\n        for _, pattern in patterns:\n            severity_str = pattern.severity.value\n            severity_counts[severity_str] = severity_counts.get(severity_str, 0) + 1\n        \n        # Generate recommendations\n        recommendations = self._generate_recommendations(patterns, context)\n        \n        # Determine if human review is required\n        requires_review = self._requires_human_review(patterns, total_risk_score)\n        \n        # Calculate overall confidence\n        confidence = sum(match.confidence for match in match_results) / len(match_results)\n        \n        result = RiskIdentificationResult(\n            identified_risks=match_results,\n            total_risk_score=total_risk_score,\n            highest_severity=highest_severity,\n            risk_count_by_severity=severity_counts,\n            recommendations=recommendations,\n            requires_human_review=requires_review,\n     trend = "stable"\n        if len(second_half) > len(first_half) * 1.5:\n            trend = "increasing"\n        elif len(second_half) < len(first_half) * 0.5:\n            trend = "decreasing"\n        \n        # Calculate average impact\n        avg_impact = sum(i.actual_impact for i in incidents) / len(incidents)\n        \n        return {\n            "trend": trend,\n WeightedRiskScorer:\n    """\n    Weighted risk scoring considering multiple factors.\n    """\n    \n    def __init__(self):\n        # Default weights for different factors\n        self.default_weights = {\n            "impact": 0.35,\n            "probability": 0.25,\n            "detectability": 0.15,\n            "controllability": 0.15,\n            "velocity": 0.10\n        }\n    \n    def calculate_score(\n        self,\n        impact_score: float,\n        probability_score: float,\n        detectability: float = 0.5,\n        controllability: float = 0.5,\n        velocity: float = 0.5,\n        custom_weights: Optional[Dict[str, float]] = None\n    ) -> RiskScoreBreakdown:\n        """\n        Calculate weighted risk score.\n        \n        Args:\n            impact_score: Impact score (0-10)\n            probability_score: Probability score (0-1)\n            detectability: How easily the risk can be detected (0-1)\n            controllability: How Returns:\n            RiskScoreBreakdown with calculation details\n        """\n        weights = custom_weights or self.default_weights\n        \n        # Normalize impact to 0-1 scale for calculation\n        normalized_impact = impact_score / 10.0\n        \n        # Calculate weighted score\n        factors = [\n            RiskFactor(\n                name="impact",\n                value=normalized_impact,\n                weight=weights.get("impact", 0.35),\n                description="Severity of consequences if risk occurs"\n            ),\n            RiskFactor(\n                name="probability",\n                value=probability_score,\n                weight=weights.get("probability", 0.25),\n                description="Likelihood of risk occurrence"\n ),\n            RiskFactor(\n                name="velocity",\n                value=velocity,\n                weight=weights.get("velocity", 0.10),\n                description="Speed at which risk total_score = weighted_sum * 10.0\n        \n        return RiskScoreBreakdown(\n            total_score=total_score,\n            impact_score=impact_score,\n            probability_score=probability_score,\n            factors=factors,\n            method_used=ScoringMethod.WEIGHTED,\n            confidence=0.9\n        )\n\n\nclass HistoricalRiskScorer:\n    """\n    Risk scoring based on historical incident data.\n    """\n    \n    def calculate_score(\n        self,\n        pattern: RiskPattern,\n        incidents: List[RiskIncident],\n        base_impact: float,\n        base_probability: float\n    ) -> RiskScoreBreakdown:\n        """\n        Calculate risk score adjusted by historical data.\n        \n        Args:\n            pattern: Risk pattern to score\n            incidents: Historical incidents for this pattern\n            base_impact: Base impact score\n            base_probability: Base probability score\n            \n        Returns:\n            RiskScoreBreakdown with historical adjustments\n        """\n        if not incidents:\n            # No historical data, use base scores\n            return BasicRiskScorer().calculate_score(base_impact, base_probability)\n        \n        # Calculate historical impact (average of actual impacts)\n        historical_impacts = [i.actual_impact for i in incidents]\n        avg_historical_impact = statistics.mean(historical_impacts)\n        \n        # Calculate historical probability (frequency of occurrence)\n        days_span = 365  # Look at last
