scores\n        blended_impact = 0.6 * base_impact + 0.4 * avg_historical_impact\n        blended_probability = 0.6 * base_probability + 0.4 * historical_probability\n        \n        # Calculate trend factor\n        trend_factor = self._calculate_trend_factor(incidents)\n        \n        # Adjust probability based on trend\n        adjusted_probability = blended_probability * trend_factor\n        \n        total_score = blended_impact * adjusted_probability\n        \n        factors = [\n            RiskFactor(\n                name="base_impact",\n                value=base_impact / 10.0,\n                weight=0.6,\n                description="Base impact assessment"\n            ),\n            RiskFactor(\n                name="historical_impact",\n                value=avg_historical_impact / 10.0,\n                weight=0.4,\n                description=f"Average impact from {len(incidents)} incidents"\n            ),\n            RiskFactor(\n                name="base_probability",\n                value=base_probability,\n                weight=0.6,\n                description="Base probability assessment"\n            ),\n            RiskFactor(\n                name="historical_frequency",\n                value=historical_probability,\n                weight=0.4,\n                description="Historical occurrence frequency"\n            ),\n            RiskFactor(\n                name="trend_adjustment",\n                value=trend_factor,\n                weight=1.0,\n                description="Trend-based adjustment factor"\n            )\n        ]\n        \n        return RiskScoreBreakdown(\n            total_score=total_score,\n            impact_score=blended_impact,\n            probability_score=adjusted_probability,\n            factors=factors,\n            method_used=ScoringMethod.HISTORICAL,\n            confidence=0.85\n        )\n    \n    def _calculate_trend_factor(self, incidents: List[RiskIncident]) -> float:\n        """Calculate trend adjustment factor."""\n        if len(incidents) < 2:\n            return 1.0\n        \n        # Sort by date\n        sorted_incidents = sorted(incidents, key=lambda i: i.occurred_at)\n        \n        # Compare first half to second half\n        mid = len(sorted_incidents) // 2\n        first_half = sorted_incidents[:mid]\n        second_half = sorted_incidents[mid:]\n        \n        if len(second_half) > len(first_half) * 1.5:\n            return 1.3  # Increasing trend\n        elif len(second_half) < len(first_half) * 0.5:\n            return 0.7  # Decreasing trend\n        else:\n            return 1.0  # Stable\n\n\nclass DynamicRiskScorer:\n    """\n    Dynamic risk scoring that adjusts based on context.\n    """\n    \n    def calculate_score(\n        self,\n        base_impact: float,\n        base_probability: float,\n        context: Dict[str, Any]\n    ) -> RiskScoreBreakdown:\n        """\n        Calculate risk score with dynamic context adjustments.\n        \n        Args:\n            base_impact: Base impact score\n            base_probability: Base probability score\n            context: Context information for adjustments\n            \n        Returns:\n            RiskScoreBreakdown with context adjustments\n        """\n        # Extract context factors\n        environment = context.get("environment", "production")\n        user_role = context.get("user_role", "user")\n        time_of_day = context.get("time_of_day", "business_hours")\n        system_load = context.get("system_load", 0.5)\n        \n        # Calculate adjustment factors\n        factors = []\n        \n        # Environment factor\n        env_factor = 1.0\n        if environment == "production":\n            env_factor = 1.3\n        elif environment == "staging":\n            env_factor = 0.8\n        elif environment == "development":\n            env_factor = 0.5\n        \n        factors.append(RiskFactor(\n            name="environment",\n            value=env_factor,\n            weight=0.3,\n            description=f"Environment: {environment}"\n        ))\n        \n        # User role factor\n        role_factor = 1.0\n        if user_role == "admin":\n            role_factor = 1.2\n        elif user_role == "power_user":\n            role_factor = 1.1\n        \n        factors.append(RiskFactor(\n            name="user_role",\n            value=role_factor,\n            weight=0.2,\n            description=f"User role: {user_role}"\n        ))\n        \n        # Time factor\n        time_factor = 1.0\n        if time_of_day == "off_hours":\n            time_factor = 1.2  # Higher risk during off-hours\n        \n        factors.append(RiskFactor(\n            name="time_of_day",\n            value=time_factor,\n            weight=0.2,\n            description=f"Time: {time_of_day}"\n        ))\n        \n        # System load factor\n        load_factor = 0.8 + (system_load * 0.4)  # 0.8 to 1.2\n        \n        factors.append(RiskFactor(\n            name="system_load",\n            value=load_factor,\n            weight=0.3,\n            description=f"System load: {system_load:.1%}"\n        ))\n        \n        # Calculate overall adjustment\n        total_adjustment = sum(f.value * f.weight for f in factors)\n        \n        # Apply adjustments\n        adjusted_impact = base_impact * total_adjustment\n        adjusted_probability = base_probability * total_adjustment\n        \n        # Ensure within bounds\n        adjusted_impact = min(adjusted_impact, 10.0)\n        adjusted_probability = min(adjusted_probability, 1.0)\n        \n        total_score = adjusted_impact * adjusted_probability\n        \n        return RiskScoreBreakdown(\n            total_score=total_score,\n            impact_score=adjusted_impact,\n            probability_score=adjusted_probability,\n            factors=factors,\n            method_used=ScoringMethod.DYNAMIC,\n            confidence=0.8\n        )\n\n\nclass CompositeRiskScorer:\n    """\n    Composite scoring that combines multiple scoring methods.\n    """\n    \n    def __init__(self):\n        self.basic_scorer = BasicRiskScorer()\n        self.weighted_scorer = WeightedRiskScorer()\n        self.historical_scorer = HistoricalRiskScorer()\n        self.dynamic_scorer = DynamicRiskScorer()\n    \n    def calculate_score(\n        self,\n        pattern: RiskPattern,\n        incidents: Optional[List[RiskIncident]] = None,\n        context: Optional[Dict[str, Any]] = None,\n        weights: Optional[Dict[str, float]] = None\n    ) -> RiskScoreBreakdown:\n        """\n        Calculate composite risk score using multiple methods.\n        \n        Args:\n            pattern: Risk pattern to score\n            incidents: Historical incidents\n            context: Context information\n            weights: Weights for combining methods\n            \n        Returns:\n            RiskScoreBreakdown with composite calculation\n        """\n        default_weights = {\n            "basic": 0.2,\n            "weighted": 0.3,\n            "historical": 0.3,\n            "dynamic": 0.2\n        }\n        method_weights = weights or default_weights\n        \n        # Calculate scores using different methods\n        basic_score = self.basic_scorer.calculate_score(\n            pattern.impact_score,\n            pattern.probability_score\n        )\n        \n        weighted_score = self.weighted_scorer.calculate_score(\n            pattern.impact_score,\n            pattern.probability_score\n        )\n        \n        # Historical score (if data available)\n        if incidents:\n            historical_score = self.historical_scorer.calculate_score(\n                pattern,\n                incidents,\n                pattern.impact_score,\n                pattern.probability_score\n            )\n        else:\n            historical_score = basic_score\n            method_weights["historical"] = 0\n            # Redistribute weight\n            method_weights["basic"] += 0.15\n            method_weights["weighted"] += 0.15\n        \n        # Dynamic score (if context available)\n        if context:\n            dynamic_score = self.dynamic_scorer.calculate_score(\n                pattern.impact_score,\n                pattern.probability_score,\n                context\n            )\n        else:\n            dynamic_score = basic_score\n            method_weights["dynamic"] = 0\n            # Redistribute weight\n            method_weights["basic"] += 0.1\n            method_weights["weighted"] += 0.1\n        \n        # Combine scores\n        composite_total = (\n            basic_score.total_score * method_weights["basic"] +\n            weighted_score.total_score * method_weights["weighted"] +\n            historical_score.total_score * method_weights["historical"] +\n            dynamic_score.total_score * method_weights["dynamic"]\n        )\n        \n        # Combine impacts\n        composite_impact = (\n            basic_score.impact_score * method_weights["basic"] +\n            weighted_score.impact_score * method_weights["weighted"] +\n            historical_score.impact_score * method_weights["historical"] +\n            dynamic_score.impact_score * method_weights["dynamic"]\n        )\n        \n        # Combine probabilities\n        composite_probability = (\n            basic_score.probability_score * method_weights["basic"] +\n            weighted_score.probability_score * method_weights["weighted"] +\n            historical_score.probability_score * method_weights["historical"] +\n            dynamic_score.probability_score * method_weights["dynamic"]\n        )\n        \n        # Combine all factors\n        all_factors = []\n        for method_name, score in [\n            ("basic", basic_score),\n            ("weighted", weighted_score),\n            ("historical", historical_score),\n            ("dynamic", dynamic_score)\n        ]:\n            weight = method_weights.get(method_name, 0)\n            if weight > 0:\n                all_factors.append(RiskFactor(\n                    name=f"{method_name}_method",\n                    value=score.total_score / 10.0,\n                    weight=weight,\n                    description=f"Score from {method_name} method"\n                ))\n        \n        # Calculate confidence (average of method confidences)\n        confidences = [\n            basic_score.confidence * method_weights["basic"],\n            weighted_score.confidence * method_weights["weighted"],\n            historical_score.confidence * method_weights["historical"],\n            dynamic_score.confidence * method_weights["dynamic"]\n        ]\n        composite_confidence = sum(confidences)\n        \n        return RiskScoreBreakdown(\n            total_score=composite_total,\n            impact_score=composite_impact,\n            probability_score=composite_probability,\n            factors=all_factors,\n            method_used=ScoringMethod.COMPOSITE,\n            confidence=composite_confidence\n        )\n\n\nclass RiskScoringSystem:\n    """\n    Complete risk scoring system.\n    Provides unified interface for all scoring methods.\n    """\n    \n    def __init__(self):\n        self.basic_scorer = RiskScoreBreakdown with calculation details\n        """\n        if method == ScoringMethod.BASIC:\n            return self.basic_scorer.calculate_score(\n                pattern.impact_score,\n                pattern.probability_score\n            )\n        \n        elif method == ScoringMethod.WEIGHTED:\n            return self.weighted_scorer.calculate_score(\n                pattern.impact_score,\n                pattern.probability_score,\n                **kwargs\n            )\n        \n        elif method == ScoringMethod.HISTORICAL:\n            if not incidents:\n                # Fall back to basic if no incidents\n                return self.basic_scorer.calculate_score(\n                    pattern.impact_score,\n                    pattern.probability_score\n                )\n            return self.historical_scorer.calculate_score(\n                pattern,\n                incidents,\n                pattern.impact_score,\n                pattern.probability_score\n            )\n        \n        elif method == ScoringMethod.DYNAMIC:\n            if not context:\n                context = {}\n            return self.dynamic_scorer.calculate_score(\n                pattern.impact_score,\n                pattern.probability_score,\n                context\n            )\n        \n        else:  # COMPOSITE\n            return self.composite_scorer.calculate_score(\n                pattern,\n                incidents,\n                context,\n                kwargs.get("weights")\n            )\n    \n context: Optional[Dict[str, Any]] = None\n    ) -> float:\n        """\n        Recalculate and update pattern\'s risk score.\n        \n        Args:\n            pattern: Risk pattern to update\n       breakdown = self.calculate_score(pattern, method, incidents, context)\n        \n        # Update pattern\n        pattern.risk_score = breakdown.total_score\n        pattern.impact_score = breakdown.impact_score\n        pattern.probability_score = breakdown.probability_score\n        pattern.updated_at = datetime.utcnow()\n        \n        return breakdown.total_score\n    \n    def        context\n                )\n            except Exception as e:\n                print(f"Error calculating {method.value} score: {e}")\n                continue\n        \n        return      """\n        Generate mitigation recommendations for a risk pattern.\n        \n        Args:\n            pattern: Risk pattern to mitigate\n            context: Optional context\n            \n RiskSeverity.CRITICAL:\n            return MitigationPriority.IMMEDIATE\n        \n        # High risk score = high priority\n        if pattern.risk_score >= 7.0:\n            return MitigationPriority.HIGH\n        \n        # Medium risk score = medium priority\n        if pattern.risk_score >= 4.0:\n            return MitigationPriority.MEDIUM\n        \n        # Low risk score but high effectiveness = medium priority\n        if strategy.effectiveness >= 0.8:\n            return MitigationPriority.MEDIUM\n        \n        # Low risk score = low priority\n        if pattern.risk_score >= 2.0:\n            return MitigationPriority.LOW\n        \n        return MitigationPriority.OPTIONAL\n    \n    def _determine_approach(\n        self,\n        pattern: effectiveness suggests monitoring\n        if strategy.effectiveness < 0.5:\n            return MitigationApproach.MONITOR\n        \n        # Default to reduce\n        return risk reduction."""\n        # Risk reduction = current risk × strategy effectiveness\n        current_risk = pattern.risk_score / 10.0\n        reduction = current_risk * strategy.effectiveness\n        return min(reduction, 1.0)\n    \n    def _calculate_cost_benefit(\n        self,\n        strategy: MitigationStrategy,\n        risk_reduction: float,\n        current_risk_score: float\n    ) -> float:\n        """Calculate cost-benefit ratio."""\n        if not strategy.cost or strategy.cost == 0:\n            return float(\'inf\')  # Infinite benefit if no cost\n        \n        # Benefit = risk reduction × risk score\n        benefit = risk_reduction * current_risk_score * 1000  # Scale to dollars\n        \n        return benefit / strategy.cost\n    \n    def _determine_complexity(self, strategy: MitigationStrategy) -> str:\n        """Determine implementation complexity."""\n        if not strategy.implementation_time_hours:\n            return "medium"\n        \n        if strategy.implementation_time_hours <= 4:\n            return "low"\n        elif strategy.implementation_time_hours <= 16:\n            return "medium"\n        else:\n            return "high"\n    \n    def _check_prerequisites(\n        self,\n        strategy: MitigationStrategy,\n        context: Dict[str, Any]\n    ) -> bool:\n        """Check if prerequisites are met."""\n        if not strategy.prerequisites:\n            return True\n        \n        available_resources = context.get("available_resources", [])\n        \n        for prereq in pattern: RiskPattern,\n        strategy: MitigationStrategy,\n        priority: MitigationPriority,\n        approach: MitigationApproach\n    ) -> str:\n        """Generate reasoning for the recommendation."""\n        parts = []\n        \n        # Risk context\n        parts.append(\n            f"Risk \'{pattern.name}\' has {pattern.severity.value} severity "\n            f"with risk score of {pattern.risk_score:.1f}/10."\n        )\n        \n        # Strategy effectiveness\n        parts.append(\n            f"Strategy \'{strategy.name}\' has {strategy.effectiveness:.0%} effectiveness "\n            f"and can reduce risk by approximately {strategy.effectiveness * pattern.risk_score:.1f} points."\n        )\n        \n        # Priority reasoning\n        if priority == MitigationPriority.IMMEDIATE:\n            parts.append("Immediate action required due to critical severity.")\n        elif priority == MitigationPriority.HIGH:\n            parts.append("High priority due to significant risk score.")\n        \n        # Approach reasoning\n        if approach == MitigationApproach.AVOID:\n            parts.append("Recommended approach: Eliminate the risk entirely.")\n        elif approach == MitigationApproach.REDUCE:\n            parts.append("Recommended approach: Reduce likelihood or impact.")\n        \n        return " ".join(parts)\n    \n    def _find_alternatives(\n        self,\n        all_strategies: List[MitigationStrategy],\n        current_strategy: MitigationStrategy\n    ) -> List[str]:\n        """Find alternative   if abs(strategy.effectiveness - current_strategy.effectiveness) < 0.2:\n                    alternatives.append(strategy.name)\n        \n        return alternatives[:3]  # Return top 3 alternatives\n\n\nclass MitigationPlanGenerator:\n    """\n    Generates comprehensive mitigation plans for multiple risks.\n    """\n    \n    def __init__(self, recommender:  def optimize_plan(\n        self,\n        plan: MitigationPlan,\n        constraints: Dict[str, Any]\n    ) -> MitigationPlan:\n        """\n        Optimize mitigation plan based on constraints.\n        \n        Args:\n            plan: Original mitigation plan\n            constraints: Budget, time, or other constraints\n            \n        Returns:\n            Optimized mitigation plan\n        """\n        max_budget = constraints.get("max_budget")\n        max_time = constraints.get("max_time_hours")\n        \n        # Filter recommendations\n        optimized_recommendations = plan.recommendations\n        \n        if max_budget:\n            # Select recommendations within budget\n            optimized_recommendations = self._select_within_budget(\n                optimized_recommendations,\n                max_budget\n            )\n        \n        if max_time:\n            # Select recommendations within time constraint\n            optimized_recommendations = self._select_within_time(\n                optimized_recommendations,\n                max_time\n            )\n        \n        # Recalculate totals\n        total_cost = sum(\n            r.strategy.cost for r in optimized_recommendations\n            if r.strategy.cost\n        )\n        \n        total_time = sum(\n            r.strategy.implementation_time_hours _select_within_budget(\n        self,\n        recommendations: List[MitigationRecommendation],\n        max_budget: float\n    ) -> List[MitigationRecommendation]:\n        """Select recommendations within budget using greedy algorithm."""\n        # Sort by cost-benefit ratio\n        sorted_recs = sorted(\n            recommendations,\n            key=lambda r: r.cost_benefit_ratio,\n            reverse=True\n        )\n        \n        selected = []\n        current_cost = 0\n        \n        for rec in sorted_recs:\n            rec_cost = rec.strategy.cost or 0\n            if current_cost + rec_cost <= max_budget:\n                selected.append(rec)\n                current_cost += rec_cost\n        \n        return selected\n    \n    def _select_within_time(\n        self,\n        recommendations: List[MitigationRecommendation],\n        max_time: float\n    ) -> List[MitigationRecommendation]:\n        """Select recommendations within time constraint."""\n        # Sort by priority and risk reduction\n        sorted_recs = sorted(\n            recommendations,\n            key=lambda r: (r.priority.value, r.estimated_risk_reduction),\n ============================================================================\n# TASK 3.2: API KEY VALIDATION\n# ============================================================================\n\nclass APIKeyFormat(str, Enum):\n    """Common API key formats."""\n    ALPHANUMERIC = "alphanumeric"\n    BASE64 = "base64"\n    HEX = "hex"\n    UUID = "uuid"\n    CUSTOM = "custom"\n\n\nclass APIKeyValidationRule(BaseModel):\n    """Validation rule for API keys."""\n    name: str\n    pattern: str  # Regex pattern\n    min_length: int = 20\n    max_length: int = 100\n    format_type: APIKeyFormat = APIKeyFormat.ALPHANUMERIC\n    prefix: Optional[str] = None\n    checksum_required: bool = False\n\n\nclass APIKeyValidator:\n    """\n    Validates API keys using format rules and checksums.\n    """\n    \n    # Common API key patterns\n    PATTERNS = {\n        "github": r"^gh[ps]_[a-zA-Z0-9]{36,}$",\n        "stripe": r"^(sk|pk)_(test|live)_[a-zA-Z0-9]{24,}$",\n        "openai": r"^sk-[a-zA-Z0-9]{48}$",\n        "aws": r"^AKIA[0-9A-Z]{16}$",\n        "google": r"^AIza[0-9A-Za-z\\-_]{35}$",\n        "sendgrid": r"^SG\\.[a-zA-Z0-9_-]{22}\\.[a-zA-Z0-9_-]{43}$"\n    }\n    \n    def __init__(self):\n        self.custom_rules: Dict[str, APIKeyValidationRule] = {}\n    \n    def register_rule(self, service_name: str, rule: APIKeyValidationRule):\n        """Register a custom validation rule."""\n        self.custom_rules[service_name] = rule\n    \n    def validate_format(\n        self,\n        api_key: str,\n        service_name: Optional[str] = None\n    ) -> Tuple[bool, str]:\n        """\n        Validate API key format.\n        \n        Args:\n            api_key: API key to validate\n            service_name: Optional service name for specific validation\n            \n        Returns:\n            Tuple of (is_valid, error_message)\n        """\n        if not api_key:\n            return False, "API key is empty"\n        \n        # Check length\n        if len(api_key) < 10:\n            return False, "API key too short (minimum 10 characters)"\n        \n        if len(api_key) > 200:\n            return False, "API key too long (maximum 200 characters)"\n        \n        # Service-specific validation\n        if service_name:\n            # Check custom rules first\n            if service_name in self.custom_rules:\n                rule = self.custom_rules[service_name]\n                return self._validate_with_rule(api_key, rule)\n            \n            # Check built-in patterns\n            if service_name.lower() in self.PATTERNS:\n                pattern = self.PATTERNS[service_name.lower()]\n                if re.match(pattern, api_key):\n                    return True, ""\n                else:\n                    return False, f"Does not match {service_name} API key format"\n        \n        # Generic validation\n        return self._validate_generic(api_key)\n    \n    def _validate_with_rule(\n        self,\n        api_key: str,\n        rule: APIKeyValidationRule\n    ) -> Tuple[bool, str]:\n        """Validate using a specific rule."""\n        # Check length\n        if len(api_key) < rule.min_length:\n            return False, f"Too short (minimum {rule.min_length} characters)"\n        \n        if len(api_key) > rule.max_length:\n            return False, f"Too long (maximum {rule.max_length} characters)"\n        \n        # Check prefix\n        if rule.prefix and not api_key.startswith(rule.prefix):\n            return False, f"Must start with \'{rule.prefix}\'"\n        \n        # Check pattern\n        if not re.match(rule.pattern, api_key):\n            return False, f"Does not match required pattern"\n        \n        # Check format type\n        if rule.format_type == APIKeyFormat.BASE64:\n            if not self._is_valid_base64(api_key):\n                return False, "Invalid Base64 format"\n        \n        elif rule.format_type == APIKeyFormat.HEX:\n            if not self._is_valid_hex(api_key):\n                return False, "Invalid hexadecimal format"\n        \n        elif rule.format_type == APIKeyFormat.UUID:\n            if not self._is_valid_uuid(api_key):\n                return False, "Invalid UUID format"\n        \n        # Check checksum if required\n        if rule.checksum_required:\n            if not self._verify_checksum(api_key):\n                return False, "Invalid checksum"\n        \n        return True, ""\n    \n    def _validate_generic(self, api_key: str) -> Tuple[bool, str]:\n        """Generic API key validation."""\n        # Check for common issues\n        if api_key.isspace():\n            return False, "Contains only whitespace"\n        \n        if \' \' in api_key:\n            return False, "Contains spaces"\n        \n        # Check character set\n        if not re.match(r\'^[a-zA-Z0-9_\\-\\.]+$\', api_key):\n            return False, "Contains invalid characters"\n        \n        return True, ""\n    \n    def _is_valid_base64(self, value: str) -> bool:\n        """Check if string is valid Base64."""\n        try:\n            base64.b64decode(value, validate=True)\n            return True\n        except:\n            return False\n    \n    def _is_valid_hex(self, value: str) -> bool:\n        """Check if string is valid hexadecimal."""\n        try:\n            int(value, 16)\n            return True\n        except:\n            return False\n    \n    def _is_valid_uuid(self, value: str) -> bool:\n        """Check if string is valid UUID."""\n        uuid_pattern = r\'^[0-9a-f]{8}-[0-9a-f]{4}-[0-9a-f]{4}-[0-9a-f]{4}-[0-9a-f]{12}$\'\n        return bool(re.match(uuid_pattern, value.lower()))\n    \n    def _verify_checksum(self, api_key: str) -> bool:\n        """Verify API key checksum (if present)."""\n        # Placeholder - implement actual checksum verification\n        # This would depend on the specific checksum algorithm used\n        return True\n    \n    def generate_api_key(\n        self,\n        length: int = 32,\n        prefix: Optional[str] = None,\n        format_type: APIKeyFormat = APIKeyFormat.ALPHANUMERIC\n    ) -> str:\n        """\n        Generate a secure API key.\n        \n        Args:\n            length: Length of the key\n            prefix: Optional prefix\n            format_type: Format type for the key\n            \n        Returns:\n            Generated API key\n        """\n        import secrets\n        \n        if format_type == APIKeyFormat.BASE64:\n            key = base64.b64encode(secrets.token_bytes(length)).decode()[:length]\n        elif format_type == APIKeyFormat.HEX:\n            key = secrets.token_hex(length // 2)\n        elif format_type == APIKeyFormat.UUID:\n            import uuid\n            key = str(uuid.uuid4())\n        else:  # ALPHANUMERIC\n            alphabet = "abcdefghijklmnopqrstuvwxyzABCDEFGHIJKLMNOPQRSTUVWXYZ0123456789"\n            key = \'\'.join(secrets.choice(alphabet) for _ in range(length))\n        \n        if prefix:\n            key = f"{prefix}{key}"\n        \n        return key\n\n\n# ============================================================================\n# TASK 3.3: OAUTH TOKEN VERIFICATION\n# ============================================================================\n\nclass OAuthTokenType(str, Enum):\n    """Types of OAuth tokens."""\n    ACCESS_TOKEN = "access_token"\n    REFRESH_TOKEN = "refresh_token"\n    ID_TOKEN = "id_token"\n    BEARER_TOKEN = "bearer_token"\n\n\nclass OAuthTokenInfo(BaseModel):\n    """Information about an OAuth token."""\n    token_type: OAuthTokenType\n    expires_at: Optional[datetime] = None\n    scopes: List[str] = Field(default_factory=list)\n    issuer: Optional[str] = None\n    subject: Optional[str] = None\n    audience: Optional[str] = None\n    is_valid: bool = True\n    error: Optional[str] = None\n\n\nclass OAuthTokenVerifier:\n    """\n    Verifies OAuth tokens (JWT and opaque tokens).\n    """\n    \n    def verify_jwt_token(self, token: str) -> OAuthTokenInfo:\n        """\n        Verify JWT token structure and claims.\n        \n        Args:\n            token: JWT token string\n            \n        Returns:\n            OAuthTokenInfo with verification results\n        """\n        try:\n            # Split JWT into parts\n            parts = token.split(\'.\')\n            if len(parts) != 3:\n                return OAuthTokenInfo(\n                    token_type=OAuthTokenType.ACCESS_TOKEN,\n                    is_valid=False,\n                    error="Invalid JWT format (must have 3 parts)"\n                )\n            \n            # Decode payload (without verification for now)\n            payload = self._decode_jwt_payload(parts[1])\n            \n            if not payload:\n                return OAuthTokenInfo(\n                    token_type=OAuthTokenType.ACCESS_TOKEN,\n                    is_valid=False,\n                    error="Failed to decode JWT payload"\n                )\n            \n            # Extract claims\n            expires_at = None\n            if \'exp\' in payload:\n                expires_at = datetime.fromtimestamp(payload[\'exp\'])\n            \n            scopes = []\n            if \'scope\' in payload:\n                scopes = payload[\'scope\'].split() if isinstance(payload[\'scope\'], str) else payload[\'scope\']\n            \n            # Check expiration\n            is_valid = True\n            error = None\n            if expires_at and datetime.utcnow() > expires_at:\n                is_valid = False\n                error = "Token expired"\n            \n            return OAuthTokenInfo(\n                token_type=OAuthTokenType.ACCESS_TOKEN,\n                expires_at=expires_at,\n                scopes=scopes,\n                issuer=payload.get(\'iss\'),\n                subject=payload.get(\'sub\'),\n                audience=payload.get(\'aud\'),\n                is_valid=is_valid,\n                error=error\n            )\n        \n        except Exception as e:\n            return OAuthTokenInfo(\n                token_type=OAuthTokenType.ACCESS_TOKEN,\n                is_valid=False,\n                error=f"Verification error: {str(e)}"\n            )\n    \n    def verify_opaque_token(\n        self,\n        token: str,\n        introspection_endpoint: Optional[str] = None\n    ) -> OAuthTokenInfo:\n        """\n        Verify opaque OAuth token.\n        \n        Args:\n            token: Opaque token string\n            introspection_endpoint: Optional introspection endpoint placeholder implementation\n        \n        if not introspection_endpoint:\n            # Basic validation without introspection\n            if len(token) < 20:\n                return OAuthTokenInfo(\n                    token_type=OAuthTokenType.BEARER_TOKEN,\n                    is_valid=False,\n                    error="Token too short"\n                )\n            \n            return OAuthTokenInfo(\n                token_type=OAuthTokenType.BEARER_TOKEN,\n                is_valid=True\n            )\n        \n        # Would make HTTP request to introspection endpoint\n        # Placeholder for actual implementation\n        return OAuthTokenInfo(\n            token_type=OAuthTokenType.BEARER_TOKEN,\n            is_valid=True\n        )\n    \n    def _decode_jwt_payload(self, payload_part: str) -> Optional[Dict[str, Any]]:\n        """Decode JWT payload from Base64."""\n        try:\n            # Add padding if needed\n            padding = 4 - len(payload_part) % 4\n            if padding != 4:\n                payload_part += \'=\' * padding\n            \n            decoded = base64.urlsafe_b64decode(payload_part)\n            return json.loads(decoded)\n        except:\n            return None\n    \n    def extract_scopes(self, token: str) -> List[str]:\n        """Extract scopes from token."""\n        token_info = self.verify_jwt_token(token)\n        return token_info.scopes\n\n\n# ============================================================================\n# TASK 3.4: CREDENTIAL EXPIRY TRACKING\n# ============================================================================\n\nclass ExpiryAlert(BaseModel):\n    """Alert for expiring credential."""\n    credential_id: str\n    credential_name: str\n    expires_at: datetime\n    days_until_expiry: int\n    alert_level: str  # "warning", "urgent", "critical"\n    message: str\n\n\nclass CredentialExpiryTracker:\n    """\n    Tracks credential expiration and sends alerts.\n    """\n    \n    def __init__(self):\n        self.tracked_credentials: Dict[str, Credential] = {}\n        self.alert_thresholds = {\n            "warning": 30,  # 30 days\n            "urgent": 7,    # 7 days\n            "critical": 1   # 1 day\n        }\n        self.alerts: List[ExpiryAlert] = []\n    \n    def track_credential(self, credential: Credential):\n        """Add credential to expiry tracking."""\n        if credential.expires_at:\n            self.tracked_credentials[credential.id] = credential\n    \n    def untrack_credential(self, credential_id: str):\n        """Remove credential from tracking."""\n        if credential_id in self.tracked_credentials:\n            del self.tracked_credentials[credential_id]\n    \n    def check_expiring_credentials(self) -> List[ExpiryAlert]:\n        """\n        Check for expiring credentials and generate alerts.\n        \n        Returns:\n            List of expiry alerts\n        """\n        alerts = []\n        now = datetime.utcnow()\n        \n        for credential in self.tracked_credentials.values():\n            if not credential.expires_at:\n                continue\n            \n            days_until_expiry = (credential.expires_at - now).days\n            \n            # Determine alert level\n            alert_level = None\n            if days_until_expiry <= self.alert_thresholds["critical"]:\n                alert_level = "critical"\n            elif days_until_expiry <= self.alert_thresholds["urgent"]:\n                alert_level = "urgent"\n            elif days_until_expiry <= self.alert_thresholds["warning"]:\n                alert_level = "warning"\n            \n            if alert_level:\n                message = self._generate_alert_message(\n                    credential,\n                    days_until_expiry,\n                    alert_level\n                )\n                \n                alert = ExpiryAlert(\n                    credential_id=credential.id,\n                    credential_name=f"{credential.service_name}_{credential.credential_type}",\n                    expires_at=credential.expires_at,\n                    days_until_expiry=days_until_expiry,\n                    alert_level=alert_level,\n                    message=message\n                )\n                \n                alerts.append(alert)\n        \n        self.alerts = alerts\n        return alerts\n    \n    def get_expiring_soon(self, days: int = 30) -> List[Credential]:\n        """Get credentials expiring within specified days."""\n        cutoff = datetime.utcnow() + timedelta(days=days)\n        \n        return [\n            cred for cred in self.tracked_credentials.values()\n            if cred.expires_at and cred.expires_at <= cutoff\n        ]\n    \n    def get_expired(self) -> List[Credential]:\n        """Get expired credentials."""\n        return [\n            cred for cred in self.tracked_credentials.values()\n            if cred.is_expired()\n        ]\n    \n    def set_alert_threshold(self, level: str, days: int):\n        """Set custom alert threshold."""\n        if level in self.alert_thresholds:\n            self.alert_thresholds[level] = days\n    \n    def _generate_alert_message(\n        self,\n        credential: Credential,\n        days_until_expiry: int,\n        alert_level: str\n    ) -> str:\n        """Generate alert message."""\n        if days_until_expiry <= 0:\n            return f"EXPIRED: {credential.service_name} credential has expired"\n        elif days_until_expiry == 1:\n            return f"{alert_level.upper()}: {credential.service_name} credential expires tomorrow"\n        else:\n            return f"{alert_level.upper()}: {credential.service_name} credential expires in {days_until_expiry} days"\n\n\n# ============================================================================\n# TASK 3.5: CREDENTIAL REFRESH MECHANISMS\n# ============================================================================\n\nclass RefreshStrategy(str, Enum):\n    """Strategies for refreshing credentials."""\n    AUTOMATIC = "automatic"\n    MANUAL = "manual"\n    ON_DEMAND = "on_demand"\n    SCHEDULED = "scheduled"\n\n\nclass RefreshResult(BaseModel):\n    """Result of credential refresh operation."""\n    credential_id: str\n External Validation Service\n\n### ExternalValidationService\n\n**Purpose:** Orchestrates multiple external validators for comprehensive validation.\n\n#### Methods\n\n```python\nasync def validate(\n    validation_type: ValidationType,\n    target: str,\n    context: Dict[str, Any]\n) -> ValidationResult\n```\n\n**Parameters:**\n- `validation_type`: Type of validation (CREDENTIAL, DATA_SOURCE, DOMAIN_EXPERT, etc.)\n- `target`: Item to validate\n- `context`: Additional context for validation\n\n**Returns:** `ValidationResult` with status and confidence\n\n**Example:**\n```python\nservice = ExternalValidationService()\nresult = await service.validate(\n    ValidationType.CREDENTIAL,\n    "api_key_12345",\n    {"credential_type": "api_key", "service_name": "github"}\n)\nprint(f"Valid: {result.status == ValidationStatus.VALID}")\n```\n\n---\n\n## 2. Credential Verification System\n\n### CredentialVerificationSystem\n\n**Purpose:** Complete credential management with verification, expiry tracking, and refresh.\n\n#### Methods\n\n```python\ndef add_credential(\n    credential_type: CredentialType,\n    service_name: str,\n    credential_value: str,\n    expires_at: Optional[datetime] = None\n) -> str\n```\n\n**Parameters:**\n- `credential_type`: Type of credential (API_KEY, OAUTH_TOKEN, JWT_TOKEN, etc.)\n- `service_name`: Name of the service\n- `credential_value`: The credential string\n- `expires_at`: Optional expiration date\n\n**Returns:** Credential ID\n\n```python\nasync def verify_credential(credential_id: str) -> CredentialVerificationResult\n```\n\n**Returns:** Verification result with validity status\n\n**Example:**\n```python\nsystem = CredentialVerificationSystem()\n\n# Add credential\ncred_id = system.add_credential(\n    CredentialType.API_KEY,\n    "github",\n    "ghp_xxxxxxxxxxxx",\n    expires_at=datetime.utcnow() + timedelta(days=90)\n)\n\n# Verify\nresult = await system.verify_credential(cred_id)\nprint(f"Valid: {result.is_valid}")\n```\n\n---\n\n## 3. Historical Data Analysis System\n\n### HistoricalDataAnalysisSystem\n\n**Purpose:** Analyzes historical data to calculate UD (Uncertainty in Data).\n\n#### Methods\n\n```python\ndef record_data_point(\n    source_name: str,\n    source_type: DataSourceType,\n    quality_metrics: Dict[DataQualityMetric, float],\n    success_count: int = 0,\n    error_count: int = 0\n)\n```\n\n**Parameters:**\n- `source_name`: Name of data source\n- `source_type`: Type of source (DATABASE, API, FILE, etc.)\n- `quality_metrics`: Dictionary of quality metrics\n- `success_count`: Number of successful operations\n- `error_count`: Number of failed operations\n\n```python\ndef calculate_ud(source_name: str) -> float\n```\n\n**Returns:** UD score (0.0 to 1.0)\n\n**Example:**\n```python\nsystem = HistoricalDataAnalysisSystem()\n\n# Record data points\nsystem.record_data_point(\n    source_name="user_api",\n    source_type=DataSourceType.API,\n    quality_metrics={\n        DataQualityMetric.ACCURACY: 0.95,\n        DataQualityMetric.COMPLETENESS: 0.90\n    },\n    success_count=95,\n    error_count=5\n)\n\n# Calculate UD\nud_score = system.calculate_ud("user_api")\nprint(f"UD Score: {ud_score}")\n```\n\n---\n\n## 4. Domain Expertise System\n\n### DomainExpertiseSystem\n\n**Purpose:** Manages domain experts and calculates UA (Uncertainty in Assumptions).\n\n#### Methods\n\n```python\ndef register_expert(\n    name: str,\n    expertise_level: ExpertiseLevel,\n    domains: List[str],\n    domain_categories: List[DomainCategory],\n    years_experience: int\n) -> str\n```\n\n**Returns:** Expert ID\n\n```python\ndef calculate_ua(\n    assumption: str,\n    domain: str,\n    assumption_type: AssumptionType\n) -> float\n```\n\n**Returns:** UA score (0.0 to 1.0)\n\n**Example:**\n```python\nsystem = DomainExpertiseSystem()\n\n# Register expert\nexpert_id = system.register_expert(\n    name="Dr. Smith",\n    expertise_level=ExpertiseLevel.EXPERT,\n    domains=["software_development", "security"],\n    domain_categories=[DomainCategory.TECHNOLOGY],\n    years_experience=15\n)\n\n# Calculate UA\nua_score = system.calculate_ua(\n    assumption="All user input is validated on the client side",\n    domain="software_development",\n    assumption_type=AssumptionType.TECHNICAL\n)\nprint(f"UA Score: {ua_score}")\n```\n\n---\n\n## 5. Information Quality System\n\n### InformationQualitySystem\n\n**Purpose:** Assesses information quality and calculates UI (Uncertainty in Information).\n\n#### Methods\n\n```python\ndef add_information(\n    content: str,\n    source: InformationSource,\n    published_date: Optional[datetime] = None\n) -> str\n```\n\n**Returns:** Information ID\n\n```python\ndef calculate_ui(information_id: str) -> float\n```\n\n**Returns:** UI score (0.0 to 1.0)\n\n**Example:**\n```python\nsystem = InformationQualitySystem()\n\n# Add information\ninfo_id = system.add_information(\n    content="Python 3.11 introduces significant performance improvements...",\n    source=InformationSource.OFFICIAL_DOCUMENTATION,\n    published_date=datetime(2023, 10, 1)\n)\n\n# Calculate UI\nui_score = system.calculate_ui(info_id)\nprint(f"UI Score: {ui_score}")\n```\n\n---\n\n## 6. Resource Availability System\n\n### ResourceAvailabilitySystem\n\n**Purpose:** Monitors resources and calculates UR (Uncertainty in Resources).\n\n#### Methods\n\n```python\ndef register_resource(\n    name: str,\n    resource_type: ResourceType,\n    total_capacity: float,\n    available_capacity: float,\n    unit: ResourceUnit\n) -> str\n```\n\n**Returns:** Resource ID\n\n```python\nasync def check_availability(\n    resource_id: str,\n    required_amount: float\n) -> ResourceAvailabilityCheck\n```\n\n**Returns:** Availability check result\n\n**Example:**\n```python\nsystem = ResourceAvailabilitySystem()\n\n# Register resource\nresource_id = system.register_resource(\n    name="Production CPU",\n    resource_type=ResourceType.COMPUTE,\n    total_capacity=100.0,\n    available_capacity=75.0,\n    unit=ResourceUnit.CORES\n)\n\n# Check availability\nresult = await system.check_availability(resource_id, 20.0)\nprint(f"Available: {result.is_available}")\n```\n\n---\n\n## 7. Risk Database System\n\n### RiskPatternStorageSystem\n\n**Purpose:** Stores and retrieves risk patterns with advanced querying.\n\n#### Methods\n\n```python\ndef store_pattern(\n    name: str,\n    description: str,\n    category: RiskCategory,\n    severity: RiskSeverity,\n    likelihood: RiskLikelihood,\n    impact_score: float,\n    keywords: List[str]\n) -> str\n```\n\n**Returns:** Pattern ID\n\n```python\ndef search_patterns(query: RiskPatternQuery) -> List[RiskPattern]\n```\n\n**Returns:** List of matching patterns\n\n**Example:**\n```python\nsystem = RiskPatternStorageSystem()\n\n# Store pattern\npattern_id = system.store_pattern(\n    name="SQL Injection",\n    description="Risk of SQL injection attacks",\n    category=RiskCategory.SECURITY,\n    severity=RiskSeverity.CRITICAL,\n    likelihood=RiskLikelihood.MEDIUM,\n    impact_score=9.0,\n    keywords=["sql", "injection", "database"]\n)\n\n# Search patterns\nquery = RiskPatternQuery(\n    category=RiskCategory.SECURITY,\n    min_risk_score=5.0\n)\npatterns = system.search_patterns(query)\n```\n\n---\n\n## 8. Risk Lookup System\n\n### RiskLookupSystem\n\n**Purpose:** Fast risk identification and analysis.\n\n#### Methods\n\n```python\ndef identify_risks(\n    text: str,\n    operation: str,\n    domain: Optional[str] = None\n) -> RiskIdentificationResult\n```\n\n**Returns:** Identified risks with scores\n\n```python\ndef analyze_operation(\n    operation: str,\n    domain: Optional[str] = None\n) -> Dict[str, Any]\n```\n\n**Returns:** Comprehensive risk analysis\n\n**Example:**\n```python\nsystem = RiskLookupSystem(storage)\n\n# Identify risks\nresult = system.identify_risks(\n    text="DELETE FROM users WHERE id = ?",\n    operation="database_query",\n    domain="user_management"\n)\n\nprint(f"Total Risk Score: {result.total_risk_score}")\nprint(f"Requires Review: {result.requires_human_review}")\n```\n\n---\n\n## 9. Risk Scoring System\n\n### RiskScoringSystem\n\n**Purpose:** Calculates risk scores using multiple methods.\n\n#### Methods\n\n```python\ndef calculate_score(\n    pattern: RiskPattern,\n    method: ScoringMethod = ScoringMethod.COMPOSITE\n) -> RiskScoreBreakdown\n```\n\n**Returns:** Detailed score breakdown\n\n**Example:**\n```python\nsystem = RiskScoringSystem()\n\nbreakdown = system.calculate_score(\n    pattern,\n    method=ScoringMethod.COMPOSITE\n)\n\nprint(f"Total Score: {breakdown.total_score}")\nprint(f"Confidence: {breakdown.confidence}")\n```\n\n---\n\n## 10. Risk Mitigation System\n\n### RiskMitigationSystem\n\n**Purpose:** Generates mitigation recommendations and plans.\n\n#### Methods\n\n```python\ndef get_recommendations(\n    pattern: RiskPattern\n) -> List[MitigationRecommendation]\n```\n\n**Returns:** List of mitigation recommendations\n\n```python\ndef generate_plan(\n    patterns: List[RiskPattern]\n) -> MitigationPlan\n```\n\n**Returns:** Complete mitigation plan\n\n**Example:**\n```python\nsystem = RiskMitigationSystem()\n\n# Get recommendations\nrecommendations = system.get_recommendations(pattern)\n\nfor rec in recommendations:\n    print(f"Strategy: {rec.strategy.name}")\n    print(f"Priority: {rec.priority}")\n    print(f"Cost: ${rec.strategy.cost}")\n```\n\n---\n\n## 11. Performance Optimization System\n\n### PerformanceOptimizationSystem\n\n**Purpose:** Provides caching, monitoring, and optimization.\n\n#### Methods\n\n```python\ndef get_cached(key: str) -> Optional[Any]\ndef set_cached(key: str, value: Any, ttl: Optional[int] = None)\n```\n\n**Caching operations**\n\n```python\nasync def process_parallel(\n    items: List[Any],\n    processor: Callable\n) -> List[Any]\n```\n\n**Parallel processing**\n\n```python\ndef record_performance(name: str, value: float, unit: str = "ms")\ndef get_performance_stats() -> Dict[str, Any]\n```\n\n**Performance monitoring**\n\n**Example:**\n```python\nsystem = PerformanceOptimizationSystem()\n\n# Caching\nsystem.set_cached("user_123", user_data, ttl=300)\ncached_user = system.get_cached("user_123")\n\n# Monitoring\nsystem.record_performance("api_call", 150.0, "ms")\nstats = system.get_performance_stats()\n```\n\n---\n\n## Common Patterns\n\n### Error Handling\n\nAll async methods should be wrapped in try-except:\n\n```python\ntry:\n    result = await system.verify_credential(cred_id)\nexcept Exception as e:\n    print(f"Verification failed: {e}")\n```\n\n### Context Management\n\nUse context dictionaries for additional parameters:\n\n```python\ncontext = {\n    "environment": "production",\n    "user_role": "admin",\n    "max_budget": 10000\n}\n\nresult = system.analyze_operation(operation, context=context)\n```\n\n### Batch Operations\n\nProcess multiple items efficiently:\n\n```python\nitems = [item1, item2, item3]\nresults = await system.process_parallel(items, processor_func)\n```\n\n---\n\n## Integration Example\n\nComplete workflow using multiple systems:\n\n```python\n# Initialize systems\nhistorical = HistoricalDataAnalysisSystem()\ndomain = DomainExpertiseSystem()\ninfo = InformationQualitySystem()\nresource = ResourceAvailabilitySystem()\nrisk_storage = RiskPatternStorageSystem()\nrisk_lookup = RiskLookupSystem(risk_storage.storage)\nperformance = PerformanceOptimizationSystem()\n\n# Record historical data\nhistorical.record_data_point(\n    "api_endpoint",\n    DataSourceType.API,\n "domain", AssumptionType.TECHNICAL)\nui = info.calculate_ui(info_id)\n\n# Identify risks\nrisks = risk_lookup.identify_risks(\n    "DELETE operation",\n    "database_operation"\n)\n\n# Monitor file_path="murphy_implementation/correction/correction_model.py">\n"""\nCorrection Data Model\nDefines the structure for capturing and storing human corrections.\n"""\n\nfrom typing import Dict, List, Optional, Any, Union\nfrom datetime import datetime\nfrom enum import Enum\nfrom pydantic import BaseModel, Field\nimport uuid\n\n\nclass CorrectionType(str, Enum):\n    """Types of corrections."""\n    OUTPUT_MODIFICATION = "output_modification"\n    PARAMETER_ADJUSTMENT = "parameter_adjustment"\n    LOGIC_CORRECTION = "logic_correction"\n    VALIDATION_OVERRIDE = "validation_override"\n    ASSUMPTION_CORRECTION = "assumption_correction"\n    RISK_ASSESSMENT = "risk_assessment"\n    RESOURCE_ALLOCATION = "resource_allocation"\n    WORKFLOW_CHANGE = "workflow_change"\n\n\nclass CorrectionSeverity(str, Enum):\n    """Severity of the correction."""\n    CRITICAL = "critical"  # System would have failed\n    HIGH = "high"  # Significant error\n    MEDIUM = "medium"  # Noticeable issue\n    LOW = "low"  # Minor improvement\n    COSMETIC = "cosmetic"  # Style/formatting only\n\n\nclass CorrectionSource(str, Enum):\n    """Source of the correction."""\n    HUMAN_EXPERT = "human_expert"\n    AUTOMATED_VALIDATION = "automated_validation"\n    PEER_REVIEW = "peer_review"\n    SYSTEM_FEEDBACK = "system_feedback"\n    USER_REPORT = "user_report"\n\n\nclass CorrectionStatus(str, Enum):\n    """Status of a correction."""\n    PENDING = "pending"\n    VALIDATED = "validated"\n    APPLIED = "applied"\n    REJECTED = "rejected"\n    UNDER_REVIEW = "under_review"\n\n\nclass CorrectionContext(BaseModel):\n    """Context in which the correction was made."""\n    task_id: str\n    phase: str\n    operation: str\n    domain: Optional[str] = None\n    environment: str = "production"\n    timestamp: datetime = Field(default_factory=datetime.utcnow)\n    user_id: Optional[str] = None\n    session_id: Optional[str] = None\n    metadata: Dict[str, Any] = Field(default_factory=dict)\n\n\nclass OriginalValue(BaseModel):\n    """Original value before correction."""\n    value: Any\n    type: str\n    confidence: Optional[float] = None\n    reasoning: Optional[str] = None\n    source: Optional[str] = None\n\n\nclass CorrectedValue(BaseModel):\n    """Corrected value after human intervention."""\n    value: Any\n    type: str\n    confidence: float = Field(ge=0.0, le=1.0, default=1.0)\n    reasoning: str\n    source: CorrectionSource\n    validator_id: Optional[str] = None\n\n\nclass CorrectionDiff(BaseModel):\n    """Difference between original and corrected values."""\n    field_name: str\n    original: OriginalValue\n    corrected: CorrectedValue\n    change_type: str  # "modified", "added", "removed"\n    impact_score: float = Field(ge=0.0, le=1.0)\n    description: str\n\n\nclass CorrectionMetrics(BaseModel):\n    """Metrics associated with a correction."""\n    time_to_correct_seconds: float\n    correction_complexity: str  # "simple", "moderate", "complex"\n    affected_components: List[str] = Field(default_factory=list)\n    downstream_impacts: int = 0\n    confidence_improvement: float = 0.0\n    risk_reduction: float = 0.0\n\n\nclass LearningSignal(BaseModel):\n    """Learning signal extracted from correction."""\n    pattern_type: str\n    pattern_description: str\n    applicable_contexts: List[str] = Field(default_factory=list)\n    confidence: float = Field(ge=0.0, le=1.0)\n    frequency: int = 1\n    examples: List[str] = Field(default_factory=list)\n\n\nclass Correction(BaseModel):\n    """\n    Complete correction record.\n    Captures all information about a human correction to system output.\n    """\n    # Identity\n    id: str = Field(default_factory=lambda: str(uuid.uuid4()))\n    correction_type: CorrectionType\n    severity: CorrectionSeverity\n    status: CorrectionStatus = CorrectionStatus.PENDING\n    \n    # Context\n    context: CorrectionContext\n    \n    # Changes\n    diffs: List[CorrectionDiff]\n    \n    # Explanation\n    explanation: str\n    reasoning: str\n    alternative_approaches: List[str] = Field(default_factory=list)\n    \n    # Metrics\n    metrics: CorrectionMetrics\n    \n    # Learning\n    learning_signals: List[LearningSignal] = Field(default_factory=list)\n    \n    # Validation\n    validated_by: Optional[str] = None\n    validated_at: Optional[datetime] = None\n    validation_notes: Optional[str] = None\n    \n    # Timestamps\n    created_at: datetime = Field(default_factory=datetime.utcnow)\n    updated_at: datetime = Field(default_factory=datetime.utcnow)\n    applied_at: Optional[datetime] = None\n    \n    # Metadata\n    tags: List[str] = Field(default_factory=list)\n    related_corrections: List[str] = Field(default_factory=list)\n    metadata: Dict[str, Any] = Field(default_factory=dict)\n    \n    def calculate_impact_score(self) -> float:\n        """Calculate overall impact score of the correction."""\n        if not self.diffs:\n            return 0.0\n        \n        # Weighted average of diff impact scores\n        total_impact = sum(diff.impact_score for diff in self.diffs)\n        avg_impact = total_impact / len(self.diffs)\n        \n        # Adjust by severity\n        severity_weights = {\n            CorrectionSeverity.CRITICAL: 1.0,\n            CorrectionSeverity.HIGH: 0.8,\n            CorrectionSeverity.MEDIUM: 0.6,\n            CorrectionSeverity.LOW: 0.4,\n            CorrectionSeverity.COSMETIC: 0.2\n        }\n        \n        severity_weight = severity_weights.get(self.severity, 0.5)\n        return avg_impact * severity_weight\n    \n    def get_affected_fields(self) -> List[str]:\n        """Get list of fields that were corrected."""\n        return [diff.field_name for diff in self.diffs]\n    \n    def is_validated(self) -> bool:\n        """Check if correction has been validated."""\n        return self.status == CorrectionStatus.VALIDATED\n    \n    def is_applied(self) -> bool:\n        """Check if correction has been applied."""\n        return self.status == CorrectionStatus.APPLIED\n\n\nclass CorrectionBatch(BaseModel):\n    """\n    Batch of related corrections.\n    Used for bulk operations and pattern analysis.\n    """\n    id: str = Field(default_factory=lambda: str(uuid.uuid4()))\n    name: str\n    description: str\n    corrections: List[str]  # Correction IDs\n    created_at: datetime = Field(default_factory=datetime.utcnow)\n    created_by: str\n    tags: List[str] = Field(default_factory=list)\n    metadata: Dict[str, Any] = Field(default_factory=dict)\n\n\nclass CorrectionTemplate(BaseModel):\n    """\n    Template for common correction patterns.\n    Speeds up correction entry for recurring issues.\n    """\n    id: str = Field(default_factory=lambda: str(uuid.uuid4()))\n    name: str\n    description: str\n    correction_type: CorrectionType\n    default_severity: CorrectionSeverity\n    \n    # Template fields\n    field_templates: List[Dict[str, Any]] = Field(default_factory=list)\n    reasoning_template: str\n    tags: List[str] = Field(default_factory=list)\n    \n    # Usage stats\n    usage_count: int = 0\n    last_used: Optional[datetime] = None\n    \n    def apply_template(self, context: CorrectionContext, values: Dict[str, Any]) -> Correction:\n        """Apply template to create a new correction."""\n        diffs = []\n        \n        for field_template in self.field_templates:\n            field_name = field_template["field_name"]\n            if field_name in values:\n                diff = CorrectionDiff(\n                    field_name=field_name,\n                    original=OriginalValue(\n                        value=values.get(f"{field_name}_original"),\n                        type=field_template.get("type", "string")\n                    ),\n                    corrected=CorrectedValue(\n                        value=values[field_name],\n                        type=field_template.get("type", "string"),\n                        reasoning=self.reasoning_template,\n                        source=CorrectionSource.HUMAN_EXPERT\n                    ),\n                    change_type="modified",\n                    impact_score=field_template.get("impact_score", 0.5),\n                    description=field_template.get("description", "")\n                )\n                diffs.append(diff)\n        \n        correction = Correction(\n            correction_type=self.correction_type,\n            severity=self.default_severity,\n            context=context,\n            diffs=diffs,\n            explanation=self.description,\n            reasoning=self.reasoning_template,\n            metrics=CorrectionMetrics(\n                time_to_correct_seconds=0,\n                correction_complexity="simple"\n            ),\n            tags=self.tags\n        )\n        \n        # Update usage stats\n        self.usage_count += 1\n        self.last_used = datetime.utcnow()\n        \n        return correction\n\n\nclass CorrectionStatistics(BaseModel):\n    """Statistics about corrections."""\n    total_corrections: int = 0\n    by_type: Dict[str, int] = Field(default_factory=dict)\n    by_severity: Dict[str, int] = Field(default_factory=dict)\n    by_status: Dict[str, int] = Field(default_factory=dict)\n    average_impact_score: float = 0.0\n    average_time_to_correct: float = 0.0\n    most_corrected_fields: List[Tuple[str, int]] = Field(default_factory=list)\n    correction_rate: float = 0.0  # Corrections per task\n    validation_rate: float = 0.0  # Validated / Total\n    application_rate: float = 0.0  # Applied / Validated\n\n\nclass CorrectionQuery(BaseModel):\n    """Query for searching corrections."""\n    correction_type: Optional[CorrectionType] = None\n    severity: Optional[CorrectionSeverity] = None\n    status: Optional[CorrectionStatus] = None\n    task_id: Optional[str] = None\n    user_id: Optional[str] = None\n    start_date: Optional[datetime] = None\n    end_date: Optional[datetime] = None\n    tags: Optional[List[str]] = None\n    min_impact_score: Optional[float] = None\n    limit: int = 100\n    offset: int = 0\n\n\nclass CorrectionSummary(BaseModel):\n    """Summary of a correction for display."""\n    id: str\n    correction_type: CorrectionType\n    severity: CorrectionSeverity\n    status: CorrectionStatus\n    fields_corrected: List[str]\n    impact_score: float\n    created_at: datetime\n    explanation: str\n    tags: List[str]\n\n\n# ============================================================================\n# CORRECTION RELATIONSHIPS\n# ============================================================================\n\nclass CorrectionRelationship(BaseModel):\n    """Relationship between corrections."""\n    source_correction_id: str\n    target_correction_id: str\n    relationship_type: str  # "duplicate", "related", "supersedes", "conflicts"\n    confidence: float = Field(ge=0.0, le=1.0)\n    description: str\n    created_at: datetime = Field(default_factory=datetime.utcnow)\n\n\nclass CorrectionCluster(BaseModel):\n    """Cluster of similar corrections."""\n    id: str = Field(default_factory=lambda: str(uuid.uuid4()))\n    name: str\n    description: str\n    correction_ids: List[str]\n    common_pattern: str\n    frequency: int\n    average_impact: float\n    created_at: datetime = Field(default_factory=datetime.utcnow)\n    tags: List[str] = Field(default_factory=list)\n\n\n# ============================================================================\n# CORRECTION EVENTS\n# ============================================================================\n\nclass CorrectionEvent(BaseModel):\n    """Event in the correction lifecycle."""\n    id: str = Field(default_factory=lambda: str(uuid.uuid4()))\n    correction_id: str\n    event_type: str  # "created", "validated", "applied", "rejected", "modified"\n    actor_id: str\n    timestamp: datetime = )\n\n\ndef merge_corrections(corrections: List[Correction]) -> Correction:\n    """\n    Merge multiple corrections into a single correction.\n    \n    Args:\n        corrections: List of corrections        return corrections[0]\n    \n    # Use first correction as base\n    base = corrections[0]\n    \n    # Merge diffs\n    all_diffs = []\n    for correction in corrections:\n Merge tags\n    all_tags = list(set(tag for correction in corrections for tag in correction.tags))\n    \n    # Create merged correction\n    merged = Correction(\n        correction_type=base.correction_type,\n        severity=max(c.severity for c in corrections),\n        context=base.context,\n        diffs=all_diffs,\n        explanation=f"Merged correction from        updates: Dict[str, Any]\n    ) -> bool:\n        """\n        Update a correction.\n        \n        Args:\n            correction_id: Correction ID\n            updates: Dictionary of fields   return False\n        \n        # Update fields\n        for key, value in updates.items():\n            if hasattr(correction, key):\n                setattr(correction, key, value)\n        \n        correction.updated_at = datetime.utcnow()\n        \n        # Record event\n        event = CorrectionEvent(\n            correction_id=correction_id,\n            event_type="modified",\n     """Delete a correction."""\n        if correction_id in self.corrections:\n            correction = self.corrections[correction_id]\n            \n            # Remove from indexes\n            self.task_index[correction.context.task_id].remove(correction_id)\n            self.type_index[correction.correction_type].remove(correction_id)\n            self.severity_index[correction.severity].remove(correction_id)\n            self.status_index[correction.status].remove(correction_id)\n            \n            # Delete\n            del CorrectionQuery) -> List[Correction]:\n        """\n        Query corrections with filters.\n        \n        Args:\n            query: CorrectionQuery with filter criteria\n            \n        Returns:\n            List of matching corrections\n        """\n        # Start with all corrections\n        results = list(self.corrections.values())\n        \n        # Apply filters\n        if query.correction_type:\n            correction_ids = set(self.type_index[query.correction_type])\n            results = [c for c in results if c.id in correction_ids]\n        \n        if query.severity:\n            correction_ids = set(self.severity_index[query.severity])\n            results = [c for c in results if c.id in correction_ids]\n        \n        if query.status:\n            correction_ids = set(self.status_index[query.status])\n            results = [c for c in results if c.id in correction_ids]\n        \n        if query.task_id:\n            correction_ids = set(self.task_index[query.task_id])\n            results = [c for c in results if c.id in correction_ids]\n        \n        if query.user_id:\n            correction_ids = set(self.user_index[query.user_id])\n            results = [c for c in results if c.id in correction_ids]\n        \n        if query.start_date:\n            results = [c for c in results if c.created_at >= query.start_date]\n        \n        if query.end_date:\n            results = [c for c in results if c.created_at <= query.end_date]\n        \n        if query.tags:\n            results = [\n                c for c in results\n                if any(tag in c.tags for tag in query.tags)\n            ]\n        \n        if query.min_impact_score is not None:\n            results = [\n                c for c in results\n                if c.calculate_impact_score() >= query.min_impact_score\n            ]\n        \n        # Sort by created_at (newest first)\n        results.sort(key=lambda c: c.created_at, reverse=True)\n        \n        # Apply pagination\n        start = query.offset\n        end = start + query.limit\n        return results[start:end]\n    \n    def get_corrections_by_task(self, task_id: str) -> List[Correction]:\n        """Get all corrections for a task."""\n        correction_ids = self.task_index.get(task_id, [])\n        return       self.store = store\n    \n    def calculate_statistics(self) -> CorrectionStatistics:\n        """Calculate overall correction statistics."""\n        corrections = list(self.store.corrections.values())\n        \n        if not corrections:\n            return CorrectionStatistics()\n        \n        # Count by type\n        by_type = defaultdict(int)\n        for correction in corrections:\n            by_type[correction.correction_type.value] += 1\n        \n        # Count by severity\n        by_severity = defaultdict(int)\n        for correction in corrections:\n            by_severity[correction.severity.value] += 1\n        \n        # Count by status\n        by_status = defaultdict(int)\n        for correction in corrections:\n            by_status[correction.status.value] += 1\n        \n        # Calculate averages\n        impact_scores = [c.calculate_impact_score() for c in corrections]\n        avg_impact = sum(impact_scores) / len(impact_scores)\n        \n        times = [c.metrics.time_to_correct_seconds for c in corrections]\n        avg_time = sum(times) / len(times) if times else 0\n        \n        # Most corrected fields\n        field_counts = defaultdict(int)\n        for correction in corrections:\n            for field in correction.get_affected_fields():\n                field_counts[field] += 1\n        \n        most_corrected = sorted(\n            field_counts.items(),\n            key=lambda x: x[1],\n            reverse=True\n        )[:10]\n        \n        # Rates\n        validated = sum(1 for c in corrections if c.is_validated())\n        applied = sum(1 for c in corrections if c.is_applied())\n        \n        validation_rate = validated / len(corrections) if corrections else 0\n        application_rate = applied / validated if validated > 0 else 0\n        \n        return CorrectionStatistics(\n            total_corrections=len(corrections),\n            by_type=dict(by_type),\n            by_severity=dict(by_severity),\n            by_status=dict(by_status),\n            average_impact_score=avg_impact,\n            average_time_to_correct=avg_time,\n            most_corrected_fields=most_corrected,\n            validation_rate=validation_rate,\n            application_rate=application_rate\n        )\n    \n    def get_correction_trends(\n        self,\n        days: int = 30\n    ) -> Dict[str, Any]:\n        """Get correction trends over time."""\n        cutoff = datetime.utcnow() - timedelta(days=days)\n        corrections = [\n            c for c in self.store.corrections.values()\n            if c.created_at >= cutoff\n        ]\n        \n        if not corrections:\n            return {"trend": "no_data"}\n        \n        # Group by day\n        by_day = defaultdict(int)\n        for correction in corrections:\n            day = correction.created_at.date()\n            by_day[day] += 1\n        \n        # Calculate trend\n        days_list = sorted(by_day.keys())\n        if len(days_list) < 2:\n            return {"trend": "insufficient_data"}\n        \n        mid = len(days_list) // 2\n        first_half_avg = sum(by_day[d] for d in days_list[:mid]) / mid\n        second_half_avg = sum(by_day[d] for d in days_list[mid:]) / (len(days_list) - mid)\n        \n        if second_half_avg > first_half_avg * 1.2:\n            trend = "increasing"\n        elif second_half_avg < first_half_avg * 0.8:\n            trend = "decreasing"\n        else:\n            trend = "stable"\n        \n        return {\n            "trend": trend,\n            "daily_average": sum(by_day.values()) / len(by_day),\n            "peak_day": max(by_day.items(), key=lambda x: x[1]),\n            "total_corrections": len(corrections)\n        }\n    \n    def get_user_statistics(self, user_id: str) -> Dict[str, Any]:\n        """Get statistics for a specific user."""\n        corrections = correction_id2, similarity_score) tuples\n        """\n        duplicates = []\n        corrections = list(self.store.corrections.values())\n        \n        for i, c1 in enumerate(corrections):\n            for c2 in corrections[i+1:]:\n                similarity = self._calculate_similarity(c1, c2)\n                if similarity > 0.8:  # High similarity threshold\n                    duplicates.append((c1.id, c2.id, similarity))\n        \n        return duplicates\n    \n    def _calculate_similarity(self, c1: Correction, c2: Correction) -> float:\n        """Calculate similarity between two corrections."""\n        score = 0.0\n        \n        # Same task\n        if c1.context.task_id == c2.context.task_id:\n            score += 0.3\n        \n        # Same type\n        if c1.correction_type == c2.correction_type:\n            score += 0.2\n        \n        # Same fields corrected\n        fields1 = set(c1.get_affected_fields())\n        fields2 = set(c2.get_affected_fields())\n        if fields1 and fields2:\n            field_overlap = len(fields1 & fields2) / len(fields1 | fields2)\n            score += 0.3 * field_overlap\n        \n        # Similar reasoning\n        if c1.reasoning and c2.reasoning:\n            # Simple word overlap\n            words1 = set(c1.reasoning.lower().split())\n            words2 = set(c2.reasoning.lower().split())\n            if words1 and words2:\n                word_overlap = len(words1 & words2) / len(words1 | words2)\n                score += 0.2 * word_overlap\n        \n        return score\n\n\nclass CorrectionStorageSystem:\n    """\n    Complete correction storage system.\n    Provides unified interface for storage and analytics.\n    """\n    \n    def    issues.extend(rule_issues)\n            suggestions.extend(rule_suggestions)\n        \n        is_valid = len(issues) == 0\n        confidence = 1.0 - (len(issues) * 0.2)  # Reduce confidence for  suggestions = []\n        \n        if len(feedback.description) < 10:\n            issues.append("Description too short")\n            suggestions.append("Provide more details about the issue")\n        \n        if len(feedback.title) < 5:\n            issues.append("Title too short")\n            suggestions.append("Use a more descriptive title")\n        \n        return issues, suggestions\n    \n    def _validate_clarity(self, feedback: Feedback) -> Tuple[List[str], List[str]]:\n        """Validate feedback clarity."""\n        issues = []\n        suggestions = []\n        \n        # action_words = ["should", "could", "need", "want", "fix", "change", "add"]\n        text = feedback.description.lower()\n        \n        if not any(word in text for word in action_words):\n            suggestions.append("Clearly state what action is needed")\n        \n        return issues, suggestions\n\n\n# ============================================================================\n# TASK 2.4: FEEDBACK ANALYTICS\n# ============================================================================\n\nclass FeedbackAnalytics:\n    """Analytics for feedback data."""\n    \n    def __init__(self):\n        self.feedback_store: List[Feedback] = []\n    \n    def add_feedback(self, feedback: Feedback):\n        """Add feedback to analytics."""\n        self.feedback_store.append(feedback)\n    \n    def get_statistics(self) -> Dict[str, Any]:\n        """Get overall feedback statistics."""\n        if not self.feedback_store:\n            return {"total_feedback": 0}\n        \n        # Count by type\n        by_type = defaultdict(int)\n        for feedback in self.feedback_store:\n            by_type[feedback.feedback_type.value] += 1\n        \n        # Count by priority\n        by_priority = defaultdict(int)\n        for feedback in self.feedback_store:\n            by_priority[feedback.priority.value] += 1\n        \n        # Count by status\n        by_status = defaultdict(int)\n        for feedback in self.feedback_store:\n            by_status[feedback.status.value] += 1\n        \n        # Calculate resolution time\n        resolution_times = []\n        for feedback in self.feedback_store:\n            if feedback.resolved_at and feedback.submitted_at:\n                delta = (feedback.resolved_at - feedback.submitted_at).total_seconds() / 3600\n                resolution_times.append(delta)\n        \n        return {\n            "total_feedback": len(self.feedback_store),\n            "by_type": dict(by_type),\n            "by_priority": dict(by_priority),\n            "by_status": dict(by_status),\n            "average_resolution_time_hours": statistics.mean(resolution_times) if resolution_times else 0,\n            "pending_feedback": sum(1 for f in self.feedback_store if f.status == FeedbackStatus.SUBMITTED)\n        }\n    \n    def get_trends(self, days: int = 30) -> Dict[str, Any]:\n        """Get feedback trends."""\n        cutoff = datetime.utcnow() - timedelta(days=days)\n        recent = [f for f in self.feedback_store if f.submitted_at >= cutoff]\n        \n        if not recent:\n            return {"trend": "no_data"}\n        \n        # Group by day\n        by_day = defaultdict(int)\n        for feedback in recent:\n            day = feedback.submitted_at.date()\n            by_day[day] += 1\n        \n        # Calculate trend\n        days_list = sorted(by_day.keys())\n        if len(days_list) < 2:\n            return {"trend": "insufficient_data"}\n        \n        mid = len(days_list) // 2\n        first_half_avg = sum(by_day[d] for d in days_list[:mid]) / mid\n        second_half_avg = sum(by_day[d] for d in days_list[mid:]) / (len(days_list) - mid)\n        \n        if second_half_avg > first_half_avg * 1.2:\n            trend = "increasing"\n        elif second_half_avg < first_half_avg * 0.8:\n            trend = "decreasing"\n        else:\n            trend = "stable"\n        \n        return {\n            "trend": trend,\n            "daily_average": sum(by_day.values()) / len(by_day),\n            "total_recent": len(recent)\n        }\n    \n    def get_user_statistics(self, user_id: str) -> Dict[str, Any]:\n        """Get statistics for a specific user."""\n        user_feedback = [f for f in self.feedback_store if f.user_id == user_id]\n        \n        if not user_feedback:\n            return {"total_feedback": 0}\n        \n        by_type = defaultdict(int)\n        for feedback in user_feedback:\n            by_type[feedback.feedback_type.value] += 1\n        \n        return {\n            "total_feedback": len(user_feedback),\n            "by_type": dict(by_type),\n            "most_recent": user_feedback[-1].submitted_at.isoformat() if user_feedback else None\n        }\n    \n    def identify_common_issues(self, limit: int = 10) -> List[Tuple[str, int]]:\n        """Identify most common issues from feedback."""\n        # Extract keywords from feedback\n        word_counts = defaultdict(int)\n        \n        for feedback in self.feedback_store:\n            words = feedback.description.lower().split()\n            # Filter out common words\n            filtered_words = [w for w in words if len(w) > 4]\n            for word in filtered_words:\n                word_counts[word] += 1\n        \n        # Return top issues\n        return sorted(word_counts.items(), key=lambda x: x[1], reverse=True)[:limit]\n\n\n# score += 0.1\n        \n        # Check length\n        if len(reasoning) > 100:\n            score += 0.2\n        \n        return min(score, 1.0)\n\n\n# Remaining code self,\n        corrections: List[Correction],\n        min_frequency: int = 3\n    ) -> List[CorrectionPattern]:\n        """\n        Extract patterns from corrections.\n        \n        Args:\n            corrections: List of corrections to analyze\n            min_frequency: Minimum frequency for a pattern\n            \n        Returns:\n            List of extracted patterns\n        """\n        patterns = []\n        \n        # Extract frequent correction patterns\n        patterns.extend(self._extract_frequent_corrections(corrections, min_frequency))\n        \n        # Extract common error patterns\n        patterns.extend(self._extract_common_errors(corrections, min_frequency))\n        \n        # Extract systematic issues\n
